**JavaScript** ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÅ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ web ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá dynamic ‡¶ï‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø client-side ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç server-side ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá **JS** ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **HTML** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **CSS** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá web ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

## üßê What is JavaScript?

JavaScript ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **high-level**, **interpreted** ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **ECMAScript** ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ web ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º dynamic ‡¶ï‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ ‡¶´‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Æ, ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **HTML** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **CSS** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá web ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

## üìú History of JavaScript

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡ßß‡ßØ‡ßØ‡ß´ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá **Netscape** ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤ **Mocha**, ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º **LiveScript**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º **JavaScript**‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤ web browser ‡¶è ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø web ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø server-side ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç, mobile app ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

## ‚ú® Features of JavaScript

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶É

1. **Lightweight and Interpreted**: JavaScript ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á lightweight ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø interpret ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá compile ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

2. **Cross-platform Compatibility**: JavaScript ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶Ü‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï browser ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶´‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

3. **Dynamic Typing**: JavaScript ‡¶è ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø dynamic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

4. **Prototype-based Object Orientation**: JavaScript ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™-‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ì‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

5. **First-class Functions**: JavaScript ‡¶è ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ, ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

## üõ†Ô∏è Uses of JavaScript

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø web ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶É

- **Web Development**: web ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® form validation, dynamic ‡¶ï‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
- **Server-side Programming**: **Node.js** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá JavaScript server-side ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Mobile App Development**: **React Native** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ framework ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá mobile app ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Game Development**: JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá browser ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï game ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

## üìù JavaScript Example

‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>JavaScript Example</title>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1 id="myHeading">üëã Hello, World!</h1>
    <button onclick="changeContent()">Change Content</button>

    <script>
      function changeContent() {
        document.getElementById("myHeading").innerHTML = "Content Changed!";
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
```

‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **button** ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá **h1** element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### Output

‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø browser ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø heading ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá "üëã Hello, World!" ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø button ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá "Change Content" ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® heading ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá "Content Changed!" ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

### ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ

1. **HTML Structure**: ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **JavaScript Function**: `changeContent()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `myHeading` element ‡¶è‡¶∞ content ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§
3. **Event Handling**: button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ function ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü element ‡¶è‡¶∞ content ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

## üöÄ Single Threaded vs Multi-Threaded Language

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Single Threaded** ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ **Single Thread** ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶•‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ **call stack** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **event loop** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### Single Threaded

**Single Threaded** ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ **call stack** ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ (Single Threaded):

```javascript
function taskOne() {
  console.log("Task One is starting...");
  for (let i = 0; i < 1000000000; i++) {
    // Simulating a time-consuming task
  }
  console.log("Task One is completed.");
}

function taskTwo() {
  console.log("Task Two is starting...");
}

taskOne();
taskTwo();
```

### Output:

```
Task One is starting...
(Task One is completed after a long delay)
Task Two is starting...
```

### ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:

‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá `taskOne()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶™ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ `taskTwo()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø single-threaded ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á `taskOne()` ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ `taskTwo()` ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

### Multi-Threaded

**Multi-Threaded** ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶•‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶•‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

#### ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ (Multi-Threaded):

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá multi-threading ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ multi-threaded ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º:

```java
class TaskOne extends Thread {
    public void run() {
        System.out.println("Task One is starting...");
        for (int i = 0; i < 1000000000; i++) {
            // Simulating a time-consuming task
        }
        System.out.println("Task One is completed.");
    }
}

class TaskTwo extends Thread {
    public void run() {
        System.out.println("Task Two is starting...");
    }
}

public class MultiThreadExample {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        TaskOne t1 = new TaskOne();
        TaskTwo t2 = new TaskTwo();
        t1.start();
        t2.start();
    }
}
```

### Output:

```
Task One is starting...
Task Two is starting...
(Task One is completed after a long delay)
```

### ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:

‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, `TaskOne` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `TaskTwo` ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá `TaskTwo` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø `TaskOne` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø multi-threading ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### JavaScript ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® Single Threaded?

JavaScript ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ **Single Threaded** ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤ **browser** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Single Threaded ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ì ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßÉ‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú JavaScript ‡¶è ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶æ **call stack** ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ì ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **blocking** ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá **asynchronous** ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® **callback**, **promises**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **async/await** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ **non-blocking** ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Single Threaded** ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ **Single Thread** ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶•‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ **call stack** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **event loop** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

## üîö Conclusion

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ web ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø web ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ ‡¶Ö‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá web ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£ ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

## HTML Document ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü JavaScript ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü?

‡ß© ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶É

- Body ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡•§
- Head ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶É `script.js`

## JavaScript Can Change The Content of HTML Element

- `getElementById` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `getElementByClass` methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML Element ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ Content ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ `innerHTML` property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶É

```js
document.getElementById("codejogot").innerHTML = "Hello JavaScript";
```

## JavaScript Can Change The Value of An Attribute

- `getElementById` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `getElementByClass` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶É

```js
<button onclick="document.getElementById('myImage').src='pic_bulbon.gif'">
  Change the photo
</button>
```

## JavaScript Can Change The CSS Style

‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶É

```js
document.getElementById("demo").style.fontSize = "35px";
```

## JavaScript Variables

- Variable ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Data Store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Container.
- ‡ß™ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá JavaScript Variable Declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶É
  - Automatically
  - `let` keyword
  - `var` keyword
  - `const` keyword

Example of Automatic Declaration:

```js
x = 5;
y = 6;
z = x + y;
```

Note: Variable Declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ Good Practice.

```js
var x = 5;
var y = 6;
var z = x + y;
```

## What is Node

- Node ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **open-source**, **cross-platform**, JavaScript **runtime environment** ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° Run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø JavaScript Code ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ Web Browser ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá Web Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° Run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Node ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡¶Æ‡¶®‡•§
- Node ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Google Chrome ‡¶è‡¶∞ V8 Engine ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
- Node.js ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞-‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶° ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

## Features of Node

- **Asynchronous and Event-Driven**

  - **Non-blocking I/O:** Node.js uses non-blocking, event-driven architecture, making it efficient and suitable for real-time applications. Non-blocking I/O means that Node.js can handle many operations simultaneously without waiting for any single operation to complete.
  - **Event Loop:** Node.js operates on a single-threaded event loop, allowing it to handle multiple connections concurrently. This is particularly useful for I/O-heavy operations.

- **Single Programming Language**
  - With Node.js, developers can use JavaScript for both client-side and server-side programming. This unification of language reduces the learning curve and allows for code reuse across the stack.
- **Package Management with npm**
  - Node.js comes with npm (Node Package Manager), a package manager that provides access to a large ecosystem of reusable libraries and tools. npm makes it easy to manage dependencies and share code with other developers.
- **Scalability**
  - Node.js is designed to build scalable network applications. Its non-blocking I/O and event-driven architecture allow it to handle many concurrent connections with minimal overhead.
- **Performance**
  - Built on the V8 JavaScript engine, Node.js provides high performance and fast execution of JavaScript code. V8 compiles JavaScript into native machine code, optimizing it for speed.

## Use Cases for Node.js

- **Web Servers:** Node.js is commonly used to build web servers that can handle HTTP requests. It is especially suitable for building RESTful APIs and real-time web applications.
- **Real-Time Applications:** Applications that require real-time communication, such as chat applications, gaming servers, and collaborative tools, benefit from Node.js's event-driven architecture.
- **Single Page Applications (SPAs):** Node.js is often used in conjunction with front-end frameworks (like Angular, React, or Vue.js) to build SPAs, where the application logic is handled on the client-side and the server provides the necessary data via APIs.
- **Command-Line Tools:** Node.js can be used to create command-line tools and scripts that automate tasks, manage systems, and process data.
- **Microservices:** Node.js is well-suited for building microservices architectures due to its lightweight nature and efficient handling of concurrent requests.

Example: Building a Simple Web Server with Node.js

```js
// Load the http module to create an HTTP server.
const http = require("http");

// Configure the HTTP server to respond with "Hello, World!" to all requests.
const server = http.createServer((req, res) => {
  // Set the response HTTP header with HTTP status and Content type
  res.writeHead(200, { "Content-Type": "text/plain" });
  // Send the response body "Hello, World!"
  res.end("Hello, World!\n");
});

// Listen on port 3000 and IP address 127.0.0.1
server.listen(3000, "127.0.0.1", () => {
  console.log("Server running at http://127.0.0.1:3000/");
});
```

## Difference Between Var, Let and Const

| **Criteria**       | **Var**                                     | **Let**                                                                                      | **Const**                                         |
| ------------------ | ------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| **Scope**          | Function-scoped                             | Block-scoped                                                                                 | Block-scoped                                      |
| **Re-declaration** | Re-declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Value Update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü | Re-declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Value Update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ Let ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ C++ ‡¶è‡¶∞ Variable ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá | Re-declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ, Value-‡¶ì Update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ |

|

## JavaScript Data Types

- JavaScript ‡¶è ‡ßÆ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Data Type ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶É
  - String
  - Number
  - Bigint
  - Boolean
  - Undefined
  - Null
  - Symbol
  - Object

Examples:

```js
// Numbers:
let length = 16;
let weight = 7.5;

// Strings:
let color = "Yellow";
let lastName = "Johnson";

// Booleans
let x = true;
let y = false;

// Object:
const person = { firstName: "John", lastName: "Doe" };

// Array object:
const cars = ["Saab", "Volvo", "BMW"];

// Date object:
const date = new Date("2022-03-25");
```

- JavaScript evaluates expressions from left to right. Different sequences can produce different results:

```js
let x = 16 + 4 + "CodeJogot";
```

Output: 20CodeJogot

```js
let x = "Volvo" + 16 + 4;
```

Output: Volvo164

## JavaScript Types are Dynamic

- JavaScript has dynamic types. This means that the same variable can be used to hold different data types.

```js
let x; // Now x is undefined
x = 5; // Now x is a Number
x = "John"; // Now x is a String
```

### 1. Introduction to JavaScript Variables

JavaScript ‡¶è variables ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã memory locations ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Variables declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá **var**, **let**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **const** keywords ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø keyword JavaScript ‡¶è variables declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç behavior ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 2. Var

#### Scope of Var

**Var** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßã variable declaration method, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ function scope ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá **var** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ variable ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á function ‡¶è‡¶∞ scope ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á accessible‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá, **var** block scope ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé loop ‡¶¨‡¶æ conditionals ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ variable ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ì accessible ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
if (true) {
  var x = 10;
}
console.log(x); // Output: 10
```

- ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **x** variable block ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø block ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá accessible ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ **var** block scope maintain ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

#### Hoisting with Var

JavaScript ‡¶è **hoisting** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá **var** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ variable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç function ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã code ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá move ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, variable declaration top ‡¶è ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ initialization ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(a); // Output: undefined
var a = 5;
```

- ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, **a** variable hoist ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á console ‡¶è **undefined** ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá, **a** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® 5 assign ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 3. Let

#### Scope of Let

**Let** ES6 (ECMAScript 2015) ‡¶è introduce ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **block-scoped**‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø block ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **let** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ variable ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á block ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá accessible ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **var** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã function scope ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá, block scope ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
if (true) {
  let y = 20;
}
console.log(y); // Output: ReferenceError: y is not defined
```

- ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, **y** variable block ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç block ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø accessible ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á **ReferenceError** ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Temporal Dead Zone (TDZ)

**Let** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ variable ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶§‡ßá hoisting ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **Temporal Dead Zone** (TDZ) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá initialization ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(b); // Output: ReferenceError: Cannot access 'b' before initialization
let b = 10;
```

- ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **b** variable initialization ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á **ReferenceError** ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 4. Const

#### Scope and Mutability of Const

**Const** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã constant value declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ keyword‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **let** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã **block-scoped**, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, **const** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ variable ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶§‡ßá change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
const z = 30;
z = 40; // Output: TypeError: Assignment to constant variable
```

- ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **z** variable ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá **TypeError** ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá, **const** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá object ‡¶¨‡¶æ array declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ properties ‡¶¨‡¶æ elements ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ reference (variable ‡¶è‡¶∞ memory location) ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
const person = { name: "John" };
person.name = "Doe"; // This is allowed
console.log(person.name); // Output: "Doe"
```

- **person** object ‡¶è‡¶∞ property ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **const** variable ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ reference ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

---

### 5. Differences Between Var, Let, and Const

| Feature            | Var                               | Let                             | Const                           |
| ------------------ | --------------------------------- | ------------------------------- | ------------------------------- |
| **Scope**          | Function scope                    | Block scope                     | Block scope                     |
| **Hoisting**       | Hoisted, initialized as undefined | Hoisted, but not initialized    | Hoisted, but not initialized    |
| **Reassignable**   | Yes                               | Yes                             | No                              |
| **Re-declaration** | Allowed (even within same scope)  | Not allowed (within same scope) | Not allowed (within same scope) |

#### Explanation:

1. **Scope**: **Var** function scoped ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì, **let** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **const** block scoped‡•§
2. **Hoisting**: ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø keyword ‡¶á hoisting ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ **let** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **const** TDZ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá initialization ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
3. **Reassignable**: **var** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **let** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ variables ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ **const** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
4. **Re-declaration**: **var** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á scope ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ **let** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **const** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á scope ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶á declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 6. Best Practices for Using Var, Let, and Const

1. **Use `let` for variables that may change**: ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã variable ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá **let** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø block scope ‡¶è ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **var** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã hoisting issue ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
2. **Use `const` for constant values**: ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã variable ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá **const** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ readability ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç predictability ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Avoid using `var`**: Modern JavaScript development ‡¶è **var** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø hoisting ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç block scope ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá bugs ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 7. Conclusion

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ **var**, **let**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **const** keyword ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã variable declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ behavior ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç scope ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡•§ **Var** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã function scoped ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç hoisting ‡¶è‡¶∞ issue ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ **Let** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã block scoped ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç TDZ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ **Const** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã block scoped ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç constant value declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Modern JavaScript development ‡¶è **let** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **const** ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã **var** ‡¶è‡¶∞ limitations ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì predictable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ Proper use of these keywords ensures cleaner, safer, and more maintainable code.

## JS Operators

- ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ Mathematical ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Logical Computatioin ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### JavaScript Assignment Operator

- Assignment Operator (=) ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```js
// Assign the value 5 to x
let x = 5;
// Assign the value 2 to y
let y = 2;
// Assign the value x + y to z:
let z = x + y;
```

### JavaScript Addition Operator

- Addition Operator ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Number ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

Example:

```js
let x = 5;
let y = 2;
let z = x + y;
```

### JavaScript Multiplication Operator

- Multiplication Operator ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Numbers ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

Example:

```js
let x = 5;
let y = 2;
let z = x * y;
```

## Types of JavaScript Operators

1. Arithmetic Operators
2. Assignment Operators
3. Comparison Operators
4. Logical Operators
5. String Operators
6. Conditional (Ternary) Operator
7. Bitwise Operator
8. Type Operator

### Arithmetic Operator

Example:

```js
let a = 3;
let x = (100 + 50) * a;
```

## Assignment Operator

Example:

```js
let x = 10;
x += 5;
```

## JavaScript String Addition

```js
let text1 = "John";
let text2 = "Doe";
let text3 = text1 + " " + text2;
```

## Adding Strings and Numbers

```js
let x = 5 + 5;
let y = "5" + 5;
let z = "Hello" + 5;
```

Output:
10
55
Hello5

## JavaScript Logical Operators

![Logical and](./chapter-03/images/logical.png)

## JavaScript Bitwise Operators

- Bit operators work on 32 bits numbers.
- Any numeric operand in the operation is converted into a 32 bit number. The result is converted back to a JavaScript number.

![bitwise](./chapter-03/images/bit.png)
Image Credit: W3 School

## JavaScript Functions

- JavaScript Function ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá function keyword ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ Function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ()
- Syntax:

```js
function name(parameter1, parameter2, parameter3) {
  // code to be executed
}
```

## JavaScript Function ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü

- When an event occurs (when a user clicks a button)
- When it is invoked (called) from JavaScript code
- Automatically (self invoked)

## Function Return Mechanism

```js
// Function is called, the return value will end up in x
let x = myFunction(4, 3);

function myFunction(a, b) {
  // Function returns the product of a and b
  return a * b;
}
```

## ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø?

- ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Avoid ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

## How to Handle Standard Input and Output in VS Code for JavaScript

Example:

```js
const readline = require("readline");

// Create an interface for reading input and output
const rl = readline.createInterface({
  input: process.stdin,
  output: process.stdout,
});

// Prompt the user for input
rl.question("Enter numbers separated by spaces: ", (input) => {
  // Process the input
  const numbers = input.split(" ").map(Number);

  // For example, using the countEvenNumbers function from earlier
  function countEvenNumbers(arr) {
    let count = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
      if (arr[i] % 2 === 0) {
        count++;
      }
    }
    return count;
  }

  const evenCount = countEvenNumbers(numbers);
  console.log(`Number of even numbers: ${evenCount}`);

  // Close the input interface
  rl.close();
});
```

In Console Write:

```js
node main.js
```

Input:

```js
Enter numbers separated by spaces: 1 2 3 4 5
```

Output:

```js
Number of even numbers: 2
```

Problem-03: Write a JavaScript function to find the difference of two numbers.

Problem-04: Write a JavaScript function to find the remainder.

Problem-05: Write a JavaScript function to check if a number is positive, negative or zero.

Problem-06: Write a JavaScript function to check if a number is odd or even.

Problem-07: Write a JavaScript function to calculate the square of a number.

Problem-08: Write a JavaScript function to concatenate two strings.

Problem-09: Write a JavaScript function to find the biggest number among 3 numbers.

Problem-10: Write a JavaScript function which returns the number of even numbers in an array.

# Chapter-04: JavaScript Object

- [What is Object](#what-is-object)
- [JavaScript Primitives](#javascript-primitives)
