### 1. Introduction to Changing CSS Using DOM

**Changing CSS using DOM** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá dynamically webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ styles ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡•§ DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá JavaScript HTML elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ styles modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user interaction ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ look ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç feel ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ For example, when a user clicks a button, a paragraph's color might change, or the size of an image could be adjusted based on screen resolution.

### 2. Why Change CSS Dynamically Using DOM?

CSS dynamically change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ structure ‡¶ì layout user ‡¶è‡¶∞ interaction ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® CSS dynamically change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:

- **Real-time User Interaction:** User actions (click, hover) ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ styles ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
- **Responsive Design Enhancements:** Screen size ‡¶¨‡¶æ resolution ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ dynamically styles ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
- **Improved User Experience:** Context-sensitive feedback ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá UI ‡¶ï‡ßá more interactive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§

### 3. Accessing Elements to Change CSS

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ elements dynamically access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ styles change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### 3.1 Using `getElementById()`

`getElementById()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá HTML element ‡¶è‡¶∞ `id` attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá specific element access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ style modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<p id="myText">Change my color</p>

<script>
  let element = document.getElementById("myText");
  element.style.color = "red";
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `getElementById()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá paragraph element ‡¶è‡¶∞ color dynamically red ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### 3.2 Using `querySelector()`

`querySelector()` CSS selector ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá elements access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ styles change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<p class="content">Change my background color</p>

<script>
  let element = document.querySelector(".content");
  element.style.backgroundColor = "lightblue";
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `querySelector()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `class="content"` ‡¶∏‡¶π element ‡¶è‡¶∞ background color ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 4. Changing CSS Styles via DOM

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá HTML elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ CSS properties change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá CSS properties change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

#### 4.1 Changing Single CSS Property

HTML element ‡¶è‡¶∞ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø property ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá `style.propertyName` syntax ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<p id="textElement">Change my font size</p>

<script>
  document.getElementById("textElement").style.fontSize = "24px";
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `fontSize` property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá paragraph element ‡¶è‡¶∞ font size dynamically ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### 4.2 Changing Multiple CSS Properties

Multiple CSS properties ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<p id="textElement">Style me with multiple properties</p>

<script>
  let element = document.getElementById("textElement");
  element.style.color = "green";
  element.style.fontSize = "20px";
  element.style.border = "2px solid black";
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï CSS property ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® color, font size, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç border‡•§

#### 4.3 Adding and Removing CSS Classes

Sometimes, instead of changing individual styles directly, it's better to add or remove entire CSS classes dynamically. This allows for cleaner code management and centralized styling in CSS files.

##### Example: Adding a CSS Class

```html
<style>
  .highlight {
    background-color: yellow;
    font-weight: bold;
  }
</style>

<p id="textElement">Add class to me</p>

<script>
  let element = document.getElementById("textElement");
  element.classList.add("highlight");
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `classList.add()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá paragraph element ‡¶è `highlight` class dynamically add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ pre-defined CSS style ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá element ‡¶ï‡ßá highlight ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

##### Example: Removing a CSS Class

```html
<p id="textElement" class="highlight">Remove class from me</p>

<script>
  let element = document.getElementById("textElement");
  element.classList.remove("highlight");
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `classList.remove()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `highlight` class remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç styles automatically disappear ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 5. Real-life Example of Changing CSS Using DOM

#### Scenario: Button Click to Change Background Color

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã page ‡¶è‡¶∞ background color ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ï Background Color ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<body>
  <h2>Click the button to change background color</h2>
  <button onclick="changeBackground()">Change Background Color</button>

  <script>
    function changeBackground() {
      // Generate random values for RGB
      let a = Math.floor(Math.random() * 256);
      let b = Math.floor(Math.random() * 256);
      let c = Math.floor(Math.random() * 256);

      // Set the new random background color
      document.body.style.backgroundColor = `rgb(${a}, ${b}, ${c})`;
    }
  </script>
</body>
```

**Explanation:**

1. **Accessing Elements:** Button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ JavaScript function call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `document.body` ‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Changing CSS Dynamically:** `style.backgroundColor` property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã page ‡¶è‡¶∞ background color change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

## Creating Animation Using DOM

### Table of Contents

1. [Introduction to Creating Animation Using DOM](#introduction-to-creating-animation-using-dom)
2. [Why Use JavaScript and DOM for Animations?](#why-use-javascript-and-dom-for-animations)
3. [Basic Concepts of DOM-Based Animation](#basic-concepts-of-dom-based-animation)
4. [Creating a Simple Animation](#creating-a-simple-animation)
   - [Using `setInterval()`](#using-setinterval)
   - [Using `requestAnimationFrame()`](#using-requestanimationframe)
5. [Animating CSS Properties with DOM](#animating-css-properties-with-dom)
6. [Real-life Example of DOM Animation](#real-life-example-of-dom-animation)

### 1. Introduction to Creating Animation Using DOM

**DOM-based animations** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá HTML elements dynamically animate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ JavaScript functions ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `setInterval()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `requestAnimationFrame()` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á animations ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ size, position, color ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá visually appealing ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç interactive animations ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 2. Why Use JavaScript and DOM for Animations?

CSS animation powerful ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì, JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç DOM ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá animation ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø control ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç DOM ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá animation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **Dynamic and Interactive Animations:** User interaction ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá animations ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Precise Control:** Frame-by-frame animation control ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ speed ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç direction manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Complex Logic:** Conditional logic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç loops ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá complex animations ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 3. Basic Concepts of DOM-Based Animation

DOM-based animation ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:

1. **Accessing DOM Elements:** Animation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø HTML elements select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `getElementById()` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `querySelector()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Modifying CSS Properties:** Animation ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ CSS properties, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `top`, `left`, `transform`, `opacity`, ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Time-Based Updates:** Regular intervals ‡¶è CSS properties update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ animation effect ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `setInterval()` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `requestAnimationFrame()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 4. Creating a Simple Animation

‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá DOM-based animation ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø: `setInterval()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `requestAnimationFrame()`‡•§

#### 4.1 Using `setInterval()`

`setInterval()` function ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ (interval) ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã function ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø basic animations ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example: Moving a Box Horizontally

```html
<div
  id="box"
  style="width:50px; height:50px; background:red; position:absolute;"
></div>

<script>
  let position = 0;
  let box = document.getElementById("box");

  function moveBox() {
    position += 2;
    box.style.left = position + "px";

    if (position >= 300) {
      clearInterval(interval); // 300px position ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßå‡¶Å‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá animation ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá
    }
  }

  let interval = setInterval(moveBox, 10); // ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø 10ms ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ moveBox function call ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá
</script>
```

**Explanation:**

1. **Accessing the Element:** `getElementById()` method ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá box element ‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Updating the Position:** ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø 10ms ‡¶è box ‡¶è‡¶∞ `left` property 2px ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Stopping the Animation:** Box ‡¶è‡¶∞ position 300px ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßå‡¶Å‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá `clearInterval()` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá animation ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### 4.2 Using `requestAnimationFrame()`

`requestAnimationFrame()` method `setInterval()` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º smoother animations ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø display ‡¶è‡¶∞ refresh rate ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ animation frame execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example: Smooth Animation Using `requestAnimationFrame()`

```html
<div
  id="box"
  style="width:50px; height:50px; background:blue; position:absolute;"
></div>

<script>
  let position = 0;
  let box = document.getElementById("box");

  function moveBox() {
    position += 2;
    box.style.left = position + "px";

    if (position < 300) {
      requestAnimationFrame(moveBox); // 300px position ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßå‡¶Å‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ animation ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßá
    }
  }

  requestAnimationFrame(moveBox);
</script>
```

**Explanation:**

1. **Smooth Animation:** `requestAnimationFrame()` function recursively call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá smooth animation ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Performance-Friendly:** `requestAnimationFrame()` display refresh rate ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá sync ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá animation ‡¶è‡¶∞ performance ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### 5. Animating CSS Properties with DOM

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá DOM ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® CSS properties animate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® size, color, opacity ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

#### Example: Fading In and Out Animation

```html
<div
  id="box"
  style="width:100px; height:100px; background:green; opacity:1;"
></div>

<script>
  let opacity = 1;
  let box = document.getElementById("box");
  let fadingOut = true;

  function fadeBox() {
    if (fadingOut) {
      opacity -= 0.02;
      if (opacity <= 0) {
        fadingOut = false;
      }
    } else {
      opacity += 0.02;
      if (opacity >= 1) {
        fadingOut = true;
      }
    }

    box.style.opacity = opacity;
    requestAnimationFrame(fadeBox);
  }

  requestAnimationFrame(fadeBox);
</script>
```

Code: https://codepen.io/FarmerAbdulAlim/pen/gONZree

**Explanation:**

1. **Opacity Control:** Box ‡¶è‡¶∞ opacity ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø frame ‡¶è increment ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç decrement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ fade-in ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç fade-out effect ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Continuous Animation:** Opacity ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `requestAnimationFrame()` recursively call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 6. Real-life Example of DOM Animation

#### Scenario: Ball Bouncing Animation

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø simple bouncing ball animation ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ball ‡¶ü‡¶ø screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá bounce ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<div
  id="ball"
  style="width:50px; height:50px; background:orange; border-radius:50%; position:absolute; top:0;"
></div>

<script>
  let position = 0;
  let speed = 2;
  let direction = 1; // 1 ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá, -1 ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá
  let ball = document.getElementById("ball");

  function bounceBall() {
    position += speed * direction;
    ball.style.top = position + "px";

    if (position >= 300 || position <= 0) {
      direction *= -1; // Ball ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßå‡¶Å‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá direction ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá
    }

    requestAnimationFrame(bounceBall);
  }

  requestAnimationFrame(bounceBall);
</script>
```

**Detailed Explanation:**

1. **Bouncing Mechanism:** Ball ‡¶è‡¶∞ `top` property ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø frame ‡¶è adjust ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç direction ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ball screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßå‡¶Å‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **Smooth Animation:** `requestAnimationFrame()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ball ‡¶è‡¶∞ smooth movement ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

## DOM Events

### Table of Contents

1. [Introduction to DOM Events](#introduction-to-dom-events)
2. [Why Use DOM Events?](#why-use-dom-events)

   - [Mouse Events](#mouse-events)
   - [Keyboard Events](#keyboard-events)
   - [Form Events](#form-events)

   - [Using `addEventListener()`](#using-addeventlistener)
5. [Real-life Example of DOM Events](#real-life-example-of-dom-events)
6. [Conclusion](#conclusion)

### 1. Introduction to DOM Events

**DOM Events** ‡¶π‡¶≤ browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá interaction ‡¶è‡¶∞ response ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® actions‡•§ Events ‡¶π‡¶≤ user actions ‡¶¨‡¶æ system-triggered events ‡¶Ø‡¶æ HTML elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: user ‡¶è‡¶∞ mouse click, keyboard input, ‡¶¨‡¶æ form submit ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá DOM events handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á actions ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá specific behavior trigger ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 2. Why Use DOM Events?

DOM events ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá webpages interactive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® user ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã event trigger ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® JavaScript ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á event handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dynamically element ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ DOM events ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®:

- **User Interaction:** Button click, form submission, ‡¶¨‡¶æ input field ‡¶è typing ‡¶è‡¶∞ response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
- **Dynamic Changes:** Real-time content change, color change, ‡¶¨‡¶æ animations trigger ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
- **Form Validation:** User data validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ form submission ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡•§

### 3. Types of DOM Events

DOM events ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã event handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ common DOM events ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

#### 3.1 Mouse Events

Mouse events mouse ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ actions handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® click, double click, hover, ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

- **click:** ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® user ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã element ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **dblclick:** Double click event trigger ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **mouseover:** ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® mouse ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá hover ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **mouseout:** ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® mouse ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã element ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá move ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<button id="myButton">Click Me</button>

<script>
  document.getElementById("myButton").addEventListener("click", function () {
    alert("Button clicked!");
  });
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `click` event handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá alert message ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### 3.2 Keyboard Events

Keyboard events keyboard ‡¶è‡¶∞ key press ‡¶¨‡¶æ release ‡¶è‡¶∞ response ‡¶è trigger ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

- **keydown:** ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø key press ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **keyup:** ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø key release ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **keypress:** Key press ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá trigger ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<input type="text" id="myInput" placeholder="Type something" />

<script>
  document
    .getElementById("myInput")
    .addEventListener("keydown", function (event) {
      console.log("Key pressed: " + event.key);
    });
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `keydown` event handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® keyboard ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã key press ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, console ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á key ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### 3.3 Form Events

Form events form elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® form submission ‡¶¨‡¶æ input field ‡¶è typing‡•§

- **submit:** Form submit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º trigger ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **focus:** ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø input field ‡¶è focus ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá‡•§
- **blur:** ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø input field ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá focus ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<form id="myForm">
  Username: <input type="text" id="username" /><br />
  <input type="submit" value="Submit" />
</form>

<script>
  document
    .getElementById("myForm")
    .addEventListener("submit", function (event) {
      event.preventDefault();
      alert("Form submitted!");
    });
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `submit` event handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç form submit ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá `event.preventDefault()` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá form submission ‡¶Ü‡¶ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç alert message ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 4. Adding Event Listeners

JavaScript ‡¶è DOM events handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø event listeners add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Event listener ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü event ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø attach ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ event trigger ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 4.1 Using `addEventListener()`

The `addEventListener()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø event listener add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
element.addEventListener(event, function);
```

##### Example:

```html
<button id="myButton">Click Me</button>

<script>
  document.getElementById("myButton").addEventListener("click", function () {
    alert("Button was clicked!");
  });
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `addEventListener()` method ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá button ‡¶è‡¶∞ `click` event handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá alert message ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 5. Real-life Example of DOM Events

#### Scenario: Button Click to Toggle Background Color

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá page ‡¶è‡¶∞ background color ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá background ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá background ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<h2>Click the button to toggle background color</h2>
<button id="toggleButton">Toggle Background Color</button>

<script>
  let isBlack = false; // Initial color status

  document
    .getElementById("toggleButton")
    .addEventListener("click", function () {
      if (isBlack) {
        document.body.style.backgroundColor = "white"; // Change to white
        isBlack = false;
      } else {
        document.body.style.backgroundColor = "black"; // Change to black
        isBlack = true;
      }
    });
</script>
```

**Detailed Explanation:**

1. **Accessing Elements:** `getElementById()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `toggleButton` ‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Toggling Background Color:** Button click ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá background color ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ click ‡¶è background color ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ click ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Using Boolean for State Management:** A boolean variable `isBlack` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá color state track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ dynamically page ‡¶è‡¶∞ background color toggle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 6. Conclusion

DOM events user ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá interaction ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá DOM events handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá webpages dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç interactive ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶†‡ßá‡•§ Different types of events ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® mouse events, keyboard events, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç form events ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá real-time user interaction handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ `addEventListener()` method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá events ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ corresponding actions ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Proper DOM event handling user experience ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modern web development ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡•§

## DOM Event Listener

### Table of Contents

1. [Introduction to Event Listeners](#introduction-to-event-listeners)

   - [Using `addEventListener()`](#using-addeventlistener)

   - [Mouse Events](#mouse-events)
   - [Keyboard Events](#keyboard-events)
   - [Form Events](#form-events)
6. [Real-life Example of Event Listener](#real-life-example-of-event-listener)
7. [Conclusion](#conclusion)

### 1. Introduction to Event Listeners

**Event Listeners** ‡¶π‡¶≤ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø powerful feature, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü events ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ elements ‡¶ï‡ßá monitor ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á event trigger ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `addEventListener()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá DOM elements ‡¶è event listener attach ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø event ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡ßá (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: mouse click, key press, ‡¶¨‡¶æ form submit), ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á event ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü function ‡¶¨‡¶æ action execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 2. Why Use Event Listeners in DOM?

Event listeners ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

- **Separation of Concerns:** HTML code ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JavaScript code ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ `addEventListener()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá events directly HTML elements ‡¶è ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- **Multiple Events:** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø element ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï event attach ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Dynamic Interaction:** User interaction ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá real-time ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® button click, mouse hover, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç keyboard input ‡¶è‡¶∞ response ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ‡•§

### 3. Adding an Event Listener

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá DOM element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø event listener attach ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `addEventListener()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 3.1 Using `addEventListener()`

`addEventListener()` method DOM element ‡¶è event listener add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü event ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø callback function ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ event trigger ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
element.addEventListener(event, function);
```

- **element:** HTML element ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá event listener add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- **event:** Event type, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® 'click', 'keydown', 'mouseover' ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
- **function:** Event trigger ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá function execute ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<button id="myButton">Click Me</button>

<script>
  document.getElementById("myButton").addEventListener("click", function () {
    alert("Button was clicked!");
  });
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `addEventListener()` method ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá button element ‡¶è‡¶∞ `click` event handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® alert message ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 4. Removing an Event Listener

Event listener dynamically remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `removeEventListener()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü event ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç function ‡¶ï‡ßá target ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá event listener remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
element.removeEventListener(event, function);
```

##### Example:

```html
<button id="myButton">Click Me</button>

<script>
  function showAlert() {
    alert("Button was clicked!");
  }

  document.getElementById("myButton").addEventListener("click", showAlert);

  // Remove the event listener after 5 seconds
  setTimeout(function () {
    document.getElementById("myButton").removeEventListener("click", showAlert);
  }, 5000);
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá button ‡¶è‡¶∞ `click` event ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø event listener add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡ß´ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶™‡¶∞ `removeEventListener()` method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá event listener remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá button ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá alert message ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

### 5. Common Event Types with Event Listeners

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ events handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ common event ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá event listener attach ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

#### 5.1 Mouse Events

Mouse events user ‡¶è‡¶∞ mouse interaction handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® click, double click, hover, ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<button id="hoverButton">Hover over me</button>

<script>
  document
    .getElementById("hoverButton")
    .addEventListener("mouseover", function () {
      this.style.backgroundColor = "yellow";
    });
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `mouseover` event handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® user button ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ mouse hover ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® button ‡¶è‡¶∞ background color ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 5.2 Keyboard Events

Keyboard events user ‡¶è‡¶∞ key press ‡¶¨‡¶æ release ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá trigger ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<input type="text" id="inputField" placeholder="Type something" />

<script>
  document
    .getElementById("inputField")
    .addEventListener("keydown", function (event) {
      console.log("Key pressed: " + event.key);
    });
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `keydown` event handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® user keyboard ‡¶è‡¶∞ key press ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á key ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ console ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 5.3 Form Events

Form events form elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® form submit, input field focus, ‡¶¨‡¶æ blur‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<form id="myForm">
  <input type="text" id="username" placeholder="Enter username" /><br />
  <input type="submit" value="Submit" />
</form>

<script>
  document
    .getElementById("myForm")
    .addEventListener("submit", function (event) {
      event.preventDefault(); // Prevent form from submitting
      alert("Form is being submitted");
    });
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá form ‡¶è‡¶∞ `submit` event handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `event.preventDefault()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá form submission ‡¶Ü‡¶ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá alert message ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 6. Real-life Example of Event Listener

#### Scenario: Toggle Text Color on Button Click

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø button ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø paragraph ‡¶è‡¶∞ text color change ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá text color ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá text color ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<p id="myText">This is some text</p>
<button id="toggleButton">Toggle Text Color</button>

<script>
  let isRed = false;

  document
    .getElementById("toggleButton")
    .addEventListener("click", function () {
      let textElement = document.getElementById("myText");
      if (isRed) {
        textElement.style.color = "black"; // Change to black
        isRed = false;
      } else {
        textElement.style.color = "red"; // Change to red
        isRed = true;
      }
    });
</script>
```

**Detailed Explanation:**

1. **Accessing Elements:** Button ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç paragraph elements ‡¶ï‡ßá DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ `getElementById()` method ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Toggling Text Color:** Button click ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá paragraph ‡¶è‡¶∞ text color change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá color ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ click ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
3. **State Management:** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø boolean variable `isRed` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ color state track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 7. Conclusion

DOM Event Listeners user interaction ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior dynamically control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ `addEventListener()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `removeEventListener()` methods DOM elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá events attach ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç detach ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ events, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® mouse events, keyboard events, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç form events, ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç interactive webpages ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Event listeners modern web development ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø real-time user interaction ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç webpage behavior ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡•§

### 1. Introduction to DOM Nodes

**DOM Nodes** ‡¶π‡¶≤ HTML ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç XML document ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßá represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ tree-like structure ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® component‡•§ DOM (Document Object Model) ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø element, attribute, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç content ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø node ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á nodes access ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá dynamically webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ structure ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç content modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Source: [W3Schools - DOM Navigation](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_htmldom_navigation.asp) | [W3Schools - DOM Nodes](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_htmldom_nodes.asp)

### 2. Types of DOM Nodes

DOM ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ nodes ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ HTML document ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßá represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø node ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü role ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá DOM tree ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 2.1 Element Nodes

**Element nodes** ‡¶π‡¶≤ HTML tags, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `<div>`, `<p>`, `<img>` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ HTML document ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã tags ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã element node ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá DOM tree ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Element node ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ structure ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<p>This is a paragraph.</p>
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `<p>` tag ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø element node.

#### 2.2 Attribute Nodes

**Attribute nodes** ‡¶π‡¶≤ HTML elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ attributes, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `id`, `class`, `src` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì attributes ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM tree ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ, JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá attribute values access ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Attributes ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ properties define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<img src="image.jpg" alt="Sample Image" />
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `src` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `alt` attributes ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø attribute node.

#### 2.3 Text Nodes

**Text nodes** ‡¶π‡¶≤ element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ actual content ‡¶¨‡¶æ text‡•§ Text nodes parent element node ‡¶è‡¶∞ child ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Text node ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ text ‡¶ï‡ßá represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<p>This is text content.</p>
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `This is text content.` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø text node.

#### 2.4 Comment Nodes

**Comment nodes** ‡¶π‡¶≤ HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ comment elements, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `<!-- -->` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá comment nodes ‡¶ì access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã webpage ‡¶è render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<!-- This is a comment -->
```

#### 2.5 Document Nodes

**Document nodes** ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã HTML document ‡¶è‡¶∞ root node‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã DOM tree ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ node ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø document ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø nodes ‡¶è‡¶∞ parent ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá `document` object ‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ structure ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç content manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 3. Navigating the DOM Tree

DOM tree ‡¶§‡ßá nodes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá parent, child, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç sibling relationships ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á relationships ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá nodes navigate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 3.1 Parent Node

**Parent node** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø node ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø node ‡¶ï‡ßá contain ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Parent node ‡¶è‡¶∞ child node ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ elements, text, ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ attributes ‡¶ï‡ßá represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<div>
  <p>This is a child paragraph.</p>
</div>
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `<div>` tag ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã parent node ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `<p>` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã child node‡•§

##### Accessing Parent Node:

```javascript
let paragraph = document.querySelector("p");
let parent = paragraph.parentNode;
console.log(parent); // Outputs the parent <div> element
```

#### 3.2 Child Nodes

**Child nodes** ‡¶π‡¶≤ parent element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ elements, attributes, ‡¶¨‡¶æ text content‡•§ DOM tree ‡¶§‡ßá parent node ‡¶è‡¶∞ child nodes ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã parent node ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶®‡ßá HTML structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Accessing Child Nodes:

```javascript
let parentElement = document.querySelector("div");
let childNodes = parentElement.childNodes; // Returns a NodeList of child nodes
console.log(childNodes);
```

#### 3.3 Sibling Nodes

**Sibling nodes** ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á parent node ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ nodes‡•§ Parent node ‡¶è‡¶∞ child nodes ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á level ‡¶è ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ sibling ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<ul>
  <li>First item</li>
  <li>Second item</li>
</ul>
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `<li>` elements ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø sibling node‡•§

##### Accessing Sibling Nodes:

```javascript
let firstItem = document.querySelector("li");
let nextSibling = firstItem.nextSibling; // Access the next sibling node
console.log(nextSibling);
```

### 4. Accessing and Manipulating DOM Nodes

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá DOM nodes access ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ commonly used DOM navigation methods ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç properties ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **`getElementById()`**: `id` attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü node access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

  ```javascript
  let element = document.getElementById("myElement");
  ```

- **`querySelector()`**: CSS selector ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ matching node return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

  ```javascript
  let firstDiv = document.querySelector("div");
  ```

- **`childNodes`**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ child nodes return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (‡¶Ø‡¶æ text ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç element nodes ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá)‡•§

  ```javascript
  let children = document.getElementById("parentDiv").childNodes;
  ```

- **`parentNode`**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø node ‡¶è‡¶∞ parent node return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

  ```javascript
  let parent = document.getElementById("childElement").parentNode;
  ```

- **`nextSibling`**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø node ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ sibling node return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

  ```javascript
  let next = document.getElementById("currentElement").nextSibling;
  ```

- **`previousSibling`**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø node ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ sibling node return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

  ```javascript
  let previous = document.getElementById("currentElement").previousSibling;
  ```

### 5. Real-life Example of DOM Node Navigation

#### Scenario: Highlighting All Paragraphs Inside a Div

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø specific `<div>` element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ `<p>` elements highlight ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ DOM nodes navigate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<div id="content">
  <p>This is the first paragraph.</p>
  <p>This is the second paragraph.</p>
  <p>This is the third paragraph.</p>
</div>

<script>
  let contentDiv = document.getElementById("content");
  let paragraphs = contentDiv.getElementsByTagName("p");

  for (let i = 0; i < paragraphs.length; i++) {
    paragraphs[i].style.backgroundColor = "yellow"; // Highlight paragraphs
  }
</script>
```

**Detailed Explanation:**

1. **Accessing Parent Element:** `getElementById()` method ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá `content` div ‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Navigating Child Nodes:** `getElementsByTagName('p')` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá div ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ `<p>` elements access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Applying Styles:** Loop ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ paragraph element ‡¶è‡¶∞ background color dynamically ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 6. Conclusion

DOM Nodes ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã HTML document ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßá represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø structure‡•§ Element nodes, attribute nodes, text nodes, comment nodes, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç document nodes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá DOM nodes access ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ content ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç structure dynamically ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Nodes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá parent-child ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç sibling relationships ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá DOM tree navigate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç interactive webpages ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶≠‡ßÇ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

## DOM Collections

### Table of Contents

1. [Introduction to DOM Collections](#introduction-to-dom-collections)

   - [HTMLCollection](#htmlcollection)
   - [NodeList](#nodelist)

5. [Accessing and Using DOM Collections](#accessing-and-using-dom-collections)
6. [Real-life Example of Using DOM Collections](#real-life-example-of-using-dom-collections)

### 1. Introduction to DOM Collections

**DOM Collections** ‡¶π‡¶≤ browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá HTML document ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá elements ‡¶¨‡¶æ nodes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø list ‡¶¨‡¶æ group‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ elements access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ collections return ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ dynamically update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á collections ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá multiple elements ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Source: [W3Schools - DOM Collections](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_htmldom_collections.asp)

### 2. Why Use DOM Collections?

DOM collections ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá access ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï elements ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á category ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á tag ‡¶¨‡¶æ class ‡¶è‡¶∞ elements, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ collection return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Collection ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 3. Common DOM Collections

DOM ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® collection type ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º:

1. **HTMLCollection**
2. **NodeList**

#### 3.1 HTMLCollection

**HTMLCollection** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø live collection ‡¶Ø‡¶æ HTML elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø list return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á collection ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá sync ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ HTMLCollection ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá document ‡¶è‡¶∞ elements, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á tag name ‡¶¨‡¶æ class name ‡¶è‡¶∞, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<ul>
  <li>Item 1</li>
  <li>Item 2</li>
  <li>Item 3</li>
</ul>

<script>
  let items = document.getElementsByTagName("li");
  console.log(items); // Outputs an HTMLCollection of <li> elements
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `getElementsByTagName('li')` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ `<li>` elements ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HTMLCollection ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### 3.2 NodeList

**NodeList** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ nodes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø list‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø static ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ live ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ NodeList ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ elements ‡¶®‡¶æ, text ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç comment nodes ‡¶ì ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ NodeList `querySelectorAll()` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá return ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø static collection ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º (‡¶è‡¶á collection ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá dynamically update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ)‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<p>This is a paragraph.</p>
<p>This is another paragraph.</p>

<script>
  let paragraphs = document.querySelectorAll("p");
  console.log(paragraphs); // Outputs a NodeList of <p> elements
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `querySelectorAll('p')` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ paragraph elements ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø NodeList ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 4. Differences Between HTMLCollection and NodeList

| Feature              | HTMLCollection                                       | NodeList                                                 |
| -------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Type of Nodes**    | Contains only element nodes                          | Can contain element nodes, text nodes, and comment nodes |
| **Live or Static**   | Always live                                          | Can be live or static (most often static)                |
| **Accessing Method** | `getElementsByClassName()`, `getElementsByTagName()` | `querySelectorAll()`                                     |
| **Iteration**        | Can iterate using `for` loop, but not `forEach`      | Can iterate using both `for` loop and `forEach`          |

### 5. Accessing and Using DOM Collections

DOM collections access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ built-in methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç collections ‡¶è‡¶∞ elements access ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç iterate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø standard loop ‡¶¨‡¶æ iteration techniques ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá HTMLCollection ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç NodeList ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

#### Example: Accessing HTMLCollection and NodeList

```html
<ul>
  <li>Item 1</li>
  <li>Item 2</li>
  <li>Item 3</li>
</ul>

<p>Paragraph 1</p>
<p>Paragraph 2</p>

<script>
  // Accessing HTMLCollection using getElementsByTagName()
  let items = document.getElementsByTagName("li");
  console.log(items); // HTMLCollection of <li> elements

  // Accessing NodeList using querySelectorAll()
  let paragraphs = document.querySelectorAll("p");
  console.log(paragraphs); // NodeList of <p> elements
</script>
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá HTMLCollection ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç NodeList ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ elements collection ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ HTMLCollection `getElementsByTagName()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá return ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç NodeList `querySelectorAll()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá return ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 6. Real-life Example of Using DOM Collections

#### Scenario: Changing the Background Color of All Paragraphs

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ paragraph elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ background color change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ DOM collections ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<p>First paragraph</p>
<p>Second paragraph</p>
<p>Third paragraph</p>

<script>
  // Get all paragraphs using querySelectorAll() (returns a NodeList)
  let paragraphs = document.querySelectorAll("p");

  // Loop through the NodeList and change the background color
  paragraphs.forEach(function (paragraph) {
    paragraph.style.backgroundColor = "lightblue";
  });
</script>
```

**Explanation:**

1. **Accessing Paragraphs:** `querySelectorAll('p')` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ paragraph elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø NodeList return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Changing Background Color:** `forEach()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ paragraphs ‡¶è‡¶∞ background color change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

## DOM NodeList Object

### Table of Contents

1. [Introduction to NodeList](#introduction-to-nodelist)
2. [Why Use NodeList?](#why-use-nodelist)
3. [Accessing NodeList](#accessing-nodelist)
4. [NodeList vs HTMLCollection](#nodelist-vs-htmlcollection)
5. [Properties and Methods of NodeList](#properties-and-methods-of-nodelist)
6. [Real-life Example of Using NodeList](#real-life-example-of-using-nodelist)
7. [Conclusion](#conclusion)

### 1. Introduction to NodeList

- **NodeList** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã DOM (Document Object Model) ‡¶è‡¶∞ nodes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø collection ‡¶¨‡¶æ list‡•§ NodeList ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá HTML elements, text nodes, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç comment nodes ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® JavaScript ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï element access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø NodeList return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø static ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ live ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá most commonly static NodeList ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ NodeList ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ groups ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

- NodeList is a collection of nodes (elements, text nodes, and comment nodes) in the DOM. It is similar to an array, but it is not an array. It is a collection of nodes that can be accessed using the `querySelectorAll()` method.

### 2. Why Use NodeList?

NodeList ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **Batch Manipulation:** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™, ‡¶∏‡¶¨ paragraph element ‡¶è‡¶∞ text color ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
- **Efficient Navigation:** Multiple nodes ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ properties modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§
- **Looping Over Elements:** NodeList ‡¶è‡¶∞ elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ looping ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá dynamically ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 3. Accessing NodeList

NodeList access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ common methods ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá:

- **`querySelectorAll()`**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø CSS selectors ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü elements ‡¶ï‡ßá select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø static NodeList return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Static NodeList DOM ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

  ```javascript
  let paragraphs = document.querySelectorAll("p"); // Returns a NodeList of all <p> elements
  ```

- **`getElementsByClassName()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `getElementsByTagName()`**: ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶á methods ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø live HTMLCollection return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá NodeList ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶æ live collection ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º DOM ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá automatic update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

  ```javascript
  let divs = document.getElementsByTagName("div"); // Returns a live NodeList-like HTMLCollection
  ```

### 4. NodeList vs HTMLCollection

NodeList ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç HTMLCollection ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ collection ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá:

| Feature                | NodeList                           | HTMLCollection                                       |
| ---------------------- | ---------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------- |
| **Types of Nodes**     | Element, text, comment nodes       | Only element nodes                                   |
| **Live or Static**     | Usually static                     | Always live                                          |
| **Methods for Access** | `querySelectorAll()`               | `getElementsByClassName()`, `getElementsByTagName()` |
| **Iteration**          | Can use `forEach()` and `for` loop | Can use only `for` loop                              |

### 5. Properties and Methods of NodeList

NodeList ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:

#### 5.1 Properties

- **`length`**: NodeList ‡¶è‡¶∞ total number of nodes return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

  ```javascript
  let paragraphs = document.querySelectorAll("p");
  console.log(paragraphs.length); // Outputs the number of <p> elements
  ```

#### 5.2 Methods

- **`item(index)`**: NodeList ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü index ‡¶è‡¶∞ element access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

  ```javascript
  let firstParagraph = paragraphs.item(0); // Access the first <p> element
  ```

- **`forEach()`**: NodeList ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ iterate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶á method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `for` loop ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

  ```javascript
  paragraphs.forEach(function (p) {
    p.style.color = "blue"; // Changes text color of all <p> elements to blue
  });
  ```

### 6. Real-life Example of Using NodeList

#### Scenario: Changing Text of All List Items

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ list items ‡¶è‡¶∞ text change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ NodeList ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<ul>
  <li>First item</li>
  <li>Second item</li>
  <li>Third item</li>
</ul>

<script>
  let listItems = document.querySelectorAll("li"); // Returns a NodeList of all <li> elements

  listItems.forEach(function (item, index) {
    item.textContent = "Updated item " + (index + 1); // Changes the text of each list item
  });
</script>
```

**Explanation:**

1. **Accessing List Items:** `querySelectorAll('li')` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ list items ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø NodeList return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Updating Text Content:** `forEach()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ list items ‡¶è‡¶∞ text dynamically update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 7. Conclusion

NodeList ‡¶π‡¶≤ DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø powerful object, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï nodes ‡¶¨‡¶æ elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ list return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá multiple elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `forEach()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá NodeList ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ loop ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Static ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç live NodeList ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `querySelectorAll()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá static NodeList ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ NodeList dynamically webpages ‡¶è‡¶∞ content ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡•§

## Browser Object Model (BOM)

### Table of Contents

### 1. Introduction to the Browser Object Model (BOM)

- The Browser Object Model (BOM) allows JavaScript to **"talk to"** the browser.

- **Browser Object Model (BOM)** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® components ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç functions ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø collection, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá interact ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ BOM ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ HTML document ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º; ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø parts ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: window, history, screen, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç location ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶Æ‡•§ BOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® aspects control ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user experience dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç interactive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

![BOM](./chapter-17/bom.png)
![BOM2](./chapter-17/bom2.png)

Image Courtesy: Learn With Sumit

### 2. Why Use BOM?

BOM ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **Browser Control:** BOM ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ window, tabs, history, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç other browser-specific features ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ control ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Enhanced Interaction:** User interaction ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ location, size, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç navigation history control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Cross-Browser Compatibility:** BOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá interact ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç browser-specific information retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 3. Key Objects of the BOM

BOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® objects ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá JavaScript browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá interact ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá BOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ objects ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

#### 3.1 Window Object

**Window object** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã BOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ object, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ browser window ‡¶ï‡ßá represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ global variables ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç functions window object ‡¶è‡¶∞ properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ height, width, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç position ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Common Properties and Methods:

- **`window.innerHeight`**: Browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ inner height return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`window.innerWidth`**: Browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ inner width return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`window.open()`**: ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® window ‡¶¨‡¶æ tab open ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`window.close()`**: Current window ‡¶¨‡¶æ tab close ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(window.innerWidth); // Outputs the width of the browser window
window.open("https://example.com", "_blank"); // Opens a new tab with the given URL
```

#### 3.2 Document Object

Although the **Document Object** BOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Document object HTML document ‡¶ï‡ßá represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç HTML elements access ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Common Methods:

- **`document.getElementById()`**: HTML elements access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **`document.createElement()`**: ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® HTML element ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
let title = document.getElementById("title");
console.log(title.innerText); // Outputs the text inside the element with id="title"
```

#### 3.3 Navigator Object

**Navigator object** browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ information ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user ‡¶è‡¶∞ platform ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ name, version, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user ‡¶è‡¶∞ operating system ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Common Properties:

- **`navigator.userAgent`**: User ‡¶è‡¶∞ browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç platform ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`navigator.language`**: Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ current language return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(navigator.userAgent); // Outputs the user's browser and platform information
console.log(navigator.language); // Outputs the browser's language setting
```

#### 3.4 Screen Object

**Screen object** browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ display screen ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ height, width, color depth ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Common Properties:

- **`screen.width`**: User ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ width return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`screen.height`**: User ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ height return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`screen.colorDepth`**: Screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ color depth return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (in bits).

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(screen.width); // Outputs the width of the user's screen
console.log(screen.colorDepth); // Outputs the color depth of the screen
```

#### 3.5 History Object

**History object** browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ navigation history handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø user ‡¶è‡¶∞ previously visited pages ‡¶è‡¶∞ list manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç back ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç forward navigation ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Common Methods:

- **`history.back()`**: Browser history ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ page ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **`history.forward()`**: Browser history ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ page ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
history.back(); // Navigates to the previous page in the browser's history
history.forward(); // Navigates to the next page in the browser's history
```

#### 3.6 Location Object

**Location object** current URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® operations ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® redirecting, reloading ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

##### Common Properties and Methods:

- **`location.href`**: Current page ‡¶è‡¶∞ URL return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`location.reload()`**: Current page reload ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`location.assign()`**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® URL ‡¶è redirect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(location.href); // Outputs the current URL
location.assign("https://example.com"); // Redirects the browser to a new URL
```

### 4. Real-life Example of Using BOM

#### Scenario: Redirecting User Based on Screen Width

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen width ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® page ‡¶è redirect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
if (screen.width < 600) {
  location.assign("https://m.example.com"); // Redirect to mobile version
} else {
  location.assign("https://www.example.com"); // Redirect to desktop version
}
```

**Explanation:**

1. **Accessing Screen Width:** `screen.width` property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ width check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Redirecting User:** User ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen size ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ different versions ‡¶è‡¶∞ website ‡¶è redirect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 5. Conclusion

**Browser Object Model (BOM)** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® components ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ control ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç manipulation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø efficient ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡•§ Window, document, navigator, screen, history, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç location object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá JavaScript browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® parts ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ BOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá webpages ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç responsive ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶†‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø browser-specific information ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user ‡¶è‡¶∞ environment ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® changes ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 1. Introduction to the Window Object

**Window object** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ object, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ browser window ‡¶ï‡ßá represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø global scope ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé JavaScript ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ global variables ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç functions window object ‡¶è‡¶∞ properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Window object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá JavaScript browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® features ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç functionalities control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### 2. Why Use the Window Object?

The Window object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **Global Access:** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø global object ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá window ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ global variables ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç functions window object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡•§
- **Browser Control:** Window object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ size, position, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç behavior manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Dialog and Timers:** JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ built-in dialog boxes (e.g., alert, prompt) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç timers (e.g., setTimeout, setInterval) window object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 3. Common Properties of the Window Object

#### 3.1 Window Size and Position

Window object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ size ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç position access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ layout dynamically adjust ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§

- **`innerWidth`**: Browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ inner width return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`innerHeight`**: Browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ inner height return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`outerWidth`**: Browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ outer width return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (including toolbars, scrollbars).
- **`outerHeight`**: Browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ outer height return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (including toolbars, scrollbars).

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(window.innerWidth); // Outputs the width of the inner browser window
console.log(window.outerHeight); // Outputs the height of the outer browser window
```

#### 3.2 Screen Information

Window object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ resolution ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

- **`screenX`**: Browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ horizontal position (relative to the screen) return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶≤ (pixel) ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø window.screenX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® 100 ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßã ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 100 ‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- **`screenY`**: Browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ vertical position (relative to the screen) return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø window.screenY ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® 50 ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßã ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 50 ‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶â‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßã ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶≠‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßã ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶°‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® window.screenX ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç window.screenY ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(window.screenX); // Outputs the horizontal position of the window on the screen
console.log(window.screenY); // Outputs the vertical position of the window on the screen
```

#### 3.3 Browser Information

Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø window object ‡¶è‡¶∞ properties ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

- **`navigator`**: Browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç platform ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`location`**: Current page ‡¶è‡¶∞ URL ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø location ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(window.navigator.userAgent); // Outputs the user agent string of the browser
console.log(window.location.href); // Outputs the current page URL
```

### 4. Common Methods of the Window Object

#### 4.1 Opening and Closing Windows

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® window/tab open ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç current window/tab close ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

- **`window.open()`**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® window ‡¶¨‡¶æ tab open ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`window.close()`**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® window/tab ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º (‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø script ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá open ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º)‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
// Open a new tab with a specific URL
window.open("https://example.com", "_blank");

// Close the current window (works only if the window was opened via JavaScript)
window.close();
```

#### 4.2 Timers: setTimeout() and setInterval()

Window object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è timers set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã function execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

- **`setTimeout()`**: ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`setInterval()`**: ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
// Execute a function after 3 seconds
window.setTimeout(function () {
  alert("This is executed after 3 seconds");
}, 3000);

// Execute a function every 2 seconds
let intervalId = window.setInterval(function () {
  console.log("This is executed every 2 seconds");
}, 2000);
```

#### 4.3 Dialog Boxes

Window object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá built-in dialog boxes ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: alert, confirm, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç prompt‡•§

- **`alert()`**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø simple alert message ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **`confirm()`**: User ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Yes/No type confirmation ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **`prompt()`**: User ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá input ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
// Display an alert box
window.alert("This is an alert box");

// Display a confirmation box and log the result (true/false)
let userConfirmed = window.confirm("Do you agree?");
console.log(userConfirmed);

// Display a prompt box and log the user input
let userInput = window.prompt("Enter your name:");
console.log(userInput);
```

### 5. Real-life Example of Using the Window Object

#### Scenario: Displaying a Welcome Message Based on Screen Size

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen size ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ different welcome messages ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
if (window.innerWidth < 600) {
  window.alert("Welcome to the mobile version of our site!");
} else {
  window.alert("Welcome to the desktop version of our site!");
}
```

**Explanation:**

1. **Screen Size Detection:** `window.innerWidth` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ width check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Displaying Message:** User ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen size ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® alert message ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 6. Conclusion

**Window Object** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶Æ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç global object, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ browser window ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Window object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá new window/tab open ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, dialog boxes ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç timers set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ size, screen position, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user ‡¶è‡¶∞ platform ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® operations ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Window object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá webpages ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç interactive ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶†‡ßá‡•§

### 1. Introduction to the Screen Object

**Screen Object** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ properties ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá **window.screen** object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen resolution, color depth, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç available screen area ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Screen object ‡¶è‡¶∞ properties ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá webpages dynamically screen size ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ content adjust ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### 2. Why Use the Screen Object?

Screen object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **Responsive Design:** User ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen resolution ‡¶¨‡¶æ size ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ layout dynamically adjust ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Performance Optimization:** ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® screen size ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç resolution ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ resources (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® images, videos) load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
- **Enhanced User Experience:** Screen properties ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ user-specific content load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user experience ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§

### 3. Common Properties of the Screen Object

Screen object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ properties ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã user ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:

#### 3.1 screen.width

**`screen.width`** property user ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ full width (in pixels) return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(screen.width); // Outputs the full width of the user's screen
```

#### 3.2 screen.height

**`screen.height`** property user ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ full height (in pixels) return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(screen.height); // Outputs the full height of the user's screen
```

#### 3.3 screen.availWidth

**`screen.availWidth`** property user ‡¶è‡¶∞ available screen width return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ total width ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá OS toolbars ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç taskbars ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(screen.availWidth); // Outputs the available width of the user's screen
```

#### 3.4 screen.availHeight

**`screen.availHeight`** property available screen height return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ height ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá OS toolbars ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç taskbars ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(screen.availHeight); // Outputs the available height of the user's screen
```

#### 3.5 screen.colorDepth

**`screen.colorDepth`** property screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ color resolution depth (in bits) return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø screen ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ color ‡¶è‡¶∞ bits ‡¶è‡¶∞ depth (e.g., 24, 32 bits) ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(screen.colorDepth); // Outputs the color depth of the screen (e.g., 24 or 32 bits)
```

#### 3.6 screen.pixelDepth

**`screen.pixelDepth`** property screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ pixel depth return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ resolution ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(screen.pixelDepth); // Outputs the pixel depth of the screen
```

### 4. Real-life Example of Using the Screen Object

#### Scenario: Redirecting User to a Mobile-Friendly Version Based on Screen Width

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen width ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ mobile-friendly ‡¶¨‡¶æ desktop version ‡¶è redirect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
if (screen.width < 600) {
  window.location.href = "https://m.example.com"; // Redirect to mobile version
} else {
  window.location.href = "https://www.example.com"; // Redirect to desktop version
}
```

**Explanation:**

1. **Screen Width Detection:** `screen.width` property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen width check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Conditional Redirect:** User ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen size ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ mobile ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ desktop version ‡¶è‡¶∞ webpage ‡¶è redirect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 5. Conclusion

**Window Screen Object** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø powerful tool, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user ‡¶è‡¶∞ screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç specifications ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ width, height, color depth, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç available screen size ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá webpages dynamically adjust ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç optimize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø responsive design ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç performance optimization ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® screen resolution ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ resources ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç layout load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
