### 1. Introduction to the Location Object

The **Window Location Object** browser window ‡¶è‡¶∞ current URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ **`window.location`** object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá current URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ access ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: protocol, hostname, pathname, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç hash‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø location object ‡¶è‡¶∞ methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá webpage reload, redirect, ‡¶¨‡¶æ replace ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Source: [W3Schools - Window Location](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_window_location.asp)

### 2. Why Use the Location Object?

The **Location Object** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **URL Manipulation:** Current page ‡¶è‡¶∞ URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ access ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Navigation Control:** URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá webpages redirect ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reload ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Interactive Features:** Query strings, hash values, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç path changes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá user-specific content dynamically load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 3. Common Properties of the Location Object

Location object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá current URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 3.1 location.href

**`location.href`** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã current URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ string‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ full address return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(location.href); // Outputs the full URL of the current page
```

#### 3.2 location.protocol

**`location.protocol`** property current page ‡¶è‡¶∞ protocol return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `http:` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `https:`‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(location.protocol); // Outputs the protocol (http or https)
```

#### 3.3 location.hostname

**`location.hostname`** property current page ‡¶è‡¶∞ domain name return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `example.com`‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(location.hostname); // Outputs the domain name of the page
```

#### 3.4 location.pathname

**`location.pathname`** property URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ path (domain ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá) return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ specific section represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(location.pathname); // Outputs the path after the domain
```

#### 3.5 location.search

**`location.search`** property URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ query string return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `?` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø query parameters ‡¶è‡¶∞ information handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(location.search); // Outputs the query string of the URL
```

#### 3.6 location.hash

**`location.hash`** property URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ fragment ‡¶¨‡¶æ hash portion return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `#` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Hash ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø specific section ‡¶è jump ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(location.hash); // Outputs the fragment identifier (hash) in the URL
```

### 4. Common Methods of the Location Object

Location object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ methods ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® operations ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 4.1 location.assign()

**`location.assign()`** method ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® URL ‡¶è redirect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø browser history ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® entry ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
location.assign("https://example.com"); // Redirects to the specified URL
```

#### 4.2 location.reload()

**`location.reload()`** method current page ‡¶ï‡ßá reload ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
location.reload(); // Reloads the current page
```

#### 4.3 location.replace()

**`location.replace()`** method ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® URL ‡¶è redirect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø browser history ‡¶§‡ßá entry ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ (‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá back button ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ page ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º)‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
location.replace("https://example.com"); // Redirects to a new URL and replaces the current one in the history
```

### 5. Real-life Example of Using the Location Object

#### Scenario: Redirecting to Another Page Based on Query String

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ query string ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® page ‡¶è redirect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
let queryString = location.search;

if (queryString.includes("mobile")) {
  location.assign("https://m.example.com"); // Redirect to the mobile version
} else {
  location.assign("https://www.example.com"); // Redirect to the desktop version
}
```

**Explanation:**

1. **Query String Detection:** `location.search` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá query string access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Conditional Redirect:** Query string ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá `mobile` keyword ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá user ‡¶ï‡ßá mobile version ‡¶è redirect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º desktop version ‡¶è‡•§

### 1. Introduction to the History Object

The **Window History Object** browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ current session ‡¶è‡¶∞ navigation history manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá **`window.history`** object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ back ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç forward navigation handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ History object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ previous pages ‡¶è ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ, ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ pages ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç current session ‡¶è‡¶∞ history modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

### 2. Why Use the History Object?

History object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

- **Navigation Control:** User ‡¶è‡¶∞ browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ back ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç forward button functionality JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Session History:** Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ session history access ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ back ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç forward navigation ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Smooth Navigation:** SPA (Single Page Applications) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã advanced web applications ‡¶è smooth page transitions ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø history object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 3. Common Methods of the History Object

#### 3.1 history.back()

**`history.back()`** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶ï‡ßá browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ history ‡¶§‡ßá back ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø back button ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
history.back(); // Navigates to the previous page in the session history
```

#### 3.2 history.forward()

**`history.forward()`** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ history ‡¶§‡ßá forward ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø forward button ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
history.forward(); // Navigates to the next page in the session history
```

#### 3.3 history.go()

**`history.go()`** method browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ history ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü number of steps back ‡¶¨‡¶æ forward ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Negative values ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá backward ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç positive values ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá forward navigation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
history.go(-2); // Navigates two steps back in the session history
history.go(1); // Navigates one step forward in the session history
```

### 4. History Length Property

**`history.length`** property current session ‡¶è‡¶∞ total number of entries return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé user ‡¶è‡¶∞ browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ session ‡¶è‡¶∞ total history length‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(history.length); // Outputs the number of pages in the session history
```

### 5. Real-life Example of Using the History Object

#### Scenario: Creating Custom Back and Forward Buttons

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ history control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø custom back ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç forward buttons ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<button id="backBtn">Go Back</button>
<button id="forwardBtn">Go Forward</button>

<script>
  // Back button functionality
  document.getElementById("backBtn").addEventListener("click", function () {
    history.back(); // Navigate to the previous page
  });

  // Forward button functionality
  document.getElementById("forwardBtn").addEventListener("click", function () {
    history.forward(); // Navigate to the next page
  });
</script>
```

**Explanation:**

1. **Back Button:** User ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® "Go Back" button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® `history.back()` method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ previous page ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **Forward Button:** User ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® "Go Forward" button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® `history.forward()` method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ next page ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 6. Conclusion

**Window History Object** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ tool, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ session ‡¶è‡¶∞ navigation history manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ History object ‡¶è‡¶∞ methods ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: `history.back()`, `history.forward()`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `history.go()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ back ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç forward navigation handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ History object SPA (Single Page Applications) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç complex web applications ‡¶è‡¶∞ smooth navigation ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§ History object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ browsing experience ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 1. Introduction to the Navigator Object

The **Window Navigator Object** browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user ‡¶è‡¶∞ environment ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ **`window.navigator`** object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ, version, operating system, language, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç connectivity status ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Navigator object ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ browser information ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user ‡¶è‡¶∞ platform ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá interact ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Source: [W3Schools - Window Navigator](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_window_navigator.asp)

### 2. Why Use the Navigator Object?

Navigator object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

- **Browser Detection:** User ‡¶è‡¶∞ browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç version detect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® browser-specific optimizations ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Platform Information:** User ‡¶è‡¶∞ operating system ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç device ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ cross-platform compatibility ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Language Support:** User ‡¶è‡¶∞ browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ language settings ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ localization ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç internationalization ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§
- **Connectivity Status:** User online ‡¶¨‡¶æ offline ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ network-dependent applications ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡•§

### 3. Common Properties of the Navigator Object

Navigator object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç system ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 3.1 navigator.appName

**`navigator.appName`** property browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Modern browsers ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ `"Netscape"` return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø legacy purposes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(navigator.appName); // Outputs the name of the browser (usually "Netscape")
```

#### 3.2 navigator.appVersion

**`navigator.appVersion`** property browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ version information return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç platform ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ string ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(navigator.appVersion); // Outputs version information about the browser
```

#### 3.3 navigator.userAgent

**`navigator.userAgent`** property browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ user agent string return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ browser, version, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç operating system ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø browser detect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ property‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(navigator.userAgent); // Outputs the user agent string of the browser
```

#### 3.4 navigator.platform

**`navigator.platform`** property user ‡¶è‡¶∞ operating system ‡¶¨‡¶æ platform return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø user ‡¶è‡¶∞ device ‡¶è‡¶∞ information ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `Win32` (Windows), `MacIntel` (Mac), `Linux` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(navigator.platform); // Outputs the user's platform (e.g., "Win32" or "MacIntel")
```

#### 3.5 navigator.language

**`navigator.language`** property user ‡¶è‡¶∞ browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ current language return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø user ‡¶è‡¶∞ language preferences ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ application ‡¶ï‡ßá optimize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(navigator.language); // Outputs the language setting of the browser (e.g., "en-US")
```

#### 3.6 navigator.onLine

**`navigator.onLine`** property browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ online ‡¶¨‡¶æ offline status return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø true ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá browser online ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç false ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá browser offline mode ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
if (navigator.onLine) {
  console.log("You are online");
} else {
  console.log("You are offline");
}
```

### 4. Common Methods of the Navigator Object

Navigator object ‡¶è‡¶∞ properties ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ methods ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç environment ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì advanced tasks ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

- **`navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition()`**: User ‡¶è‡¶∞ current geographic location ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º (assuming permission is granted by the user).

  ```javascript
  navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(function (position) {
    console.log("Latitude: " + position.coords.latitude);
    console.log("Longitude: " + position.coords.longitude);
  });
  ```

- **`navigator.javaEnabled()`**: Browser ‡¶è Java enabled ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

  ```javascript
  console.log(navigator.javaEnabled()); // Outputs true if Java is enabled
  ```

### 5. Real-life Example of Using the Navigator Object

#### Scenario: Displaying Browser Information to the User

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç platform ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø dynamically display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<div id="browserInfo"></div>

<script>
  let browserInfo = `
        <p><strong>Browser:</strong> ${navigator.appName}</p>
        <p><strong>Version:</strong> ${navigator.appVersion}</p>
        <p><strong>User Agent:</strong> ${navigator.userAgent}</p>
        <p><strong>Platform:</strong> ${navigator.platform}</p>
        <p><strong>Language:</strong> ${navigator.language}</p>
        <p><strong>Online Status:</strong> ${
          navigator.onLine ? "Online" : "Offline"
        }</p>
    `;

  document.getElementById("browserInfo").innerHTML = browserInfo;
</script>
```

**Explanation:**

1. **Accessing Navigator Properties:** Navigator object ‡¶è‡¶∞ properties ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç platform ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø dynamically display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Displaying Information:** Webpage ‡¶è user ‡¶è‡¶∞ browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç platform ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø dynamically ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 1. Introduction to JavaScript Timing Events

**JavaScript Timing Events** ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® events ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ functions execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Timing events ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá asynchronous JavaScript code execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü interval ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Timing events ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ **`setTimeout()`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`setInterval()`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Source: [W3Schools - JavaScript Timing Events](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_timing.asp)

### 2. Why Use Timing Events?

Timing events ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

- **Delay Execution:** Functions ‡¶¨‡¶æ code block ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Repeated Execution:** ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü interval ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ functions execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Asynchronous Programming:** Timing events ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ asynchronous behavior ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user interaction ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§
- **Efficient Animation & UI Updates:** Timed functions ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá UI elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ automatic update, animation, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç background operations ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 3. Common Timing Methods

#### 3.1 setTimeout()

**`setTimeout()`** method ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø one-time timer, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü delay ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ function execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
setTimeout(function, delay);
```

- **function:** The function to be executed after the delay.
- **delay:** The time in milliseconds to wait before executing the function.

##### Example:

```javascript
setTimeout(function () {
  console.log("Executed after 3 seconds");
}, 3000); // Executes after 3000 milliseconds (3 seconds)
```

#### 3.2 setInterval()

**`setInterval()`** method ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø recurring timer‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
setInterval(function, interval);
```

- **function:** The function to be executed repeatedly.
- **interval:** The time in milliseconds between each execution.

##### Example:

```javascript
setInterval(function () {
  console.log("This message repeats every 2 seconds");
}, 2000); // Executes every 2000 milliseconds (2 seconds)
```

#### 3.3 clearTimeout()

**`clearTimeout()`** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø previously set `setTimeout()` function cancel ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
clearTimeout(timeoutID);
```

- **timeoutID:** The ID of the timeout to be cleared, which is returned by `setTimeout()`.

##### Example:

```javascript
let timeoutID = setTimeout(function () {
  console.log("This will not be executed");
}, 5000);

// Cancels the timeout
clearTimeout(timeoutID);
```

#### 3.4 clearInterval()

**`clearInterval()`** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø previously set `setInterval()` function cancel ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
clearInterval(intervalID);
```

- **intervalID:** The ID of the interval to be cleared, which is returned by `setInterval()`.

##### Example:

```javascript
let intervalID = setInterval(function () {
  console.log("Repeating message");
}, 1000);

// Cancels the interval after 5 seconds
setTimeout(function () {
  clearInterval(intervalID);
}, 5000);
```

### 4. Real-life Example of Using Timing Events

#### Scenario: Creating a Countdown Timer

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø countdown timer ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ countdown number update ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç countdown ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø message display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<p id="countdown">10</p>

<script>
  let count = 10;
  let countdownElement = document.getElementById("countdown");

  let countdownTimer = setInterval(function () {
    count--;
    countdownElement.innerText = count;

    // When countdown reaches 0, stop the timer and display a message
    if (count === 0) {
      clearInterval(countdownTimer);
      countdownElement.innerText = "Time's up!";
    }
  }, 1000); // Updates every second (1000 milliseconds)
</script>
```

**Explanation:**

1. **setInterval() for Countdown:** `setInterval()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø 1 second ‡¶™‡¶∞ countdown value ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **clearInterval() to Stop Timer:** Countdown 0 ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßå‡¶Å‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá `clearInterval()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá timer ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø message display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 5. Conclusion

**JavaScript Timing Events** ‡¶π‡¶≤ powerful tools ‡¶Ø‡¶æ asynchronous code execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç functions ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü interval ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ `setTimeout()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `setInterval()` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá functions delay ‡¶¨‡¶æ repeatedly execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `clearTimeout()` ‡¶ì `clearInterval()` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá set timers cancel ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Timing events ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ asynchronous tasks ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® animations, countdowns, ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ delayed actions‡•§

### 1. Introduction to Cookies

**Cookies** ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ web browser ‡¶è store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Cookies ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá websites user-specific information save ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: authentication data, user preferences, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç browsing history‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá cookies create, read, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç delete ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ website ‡¶ï‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá dynamically interact ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

Source: [W3Schools - JavaScript Cookies](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_cookies.asp)

### 2. Why Use Cookies?

Cookies ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

- **User Session Management:** Cookies ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ login state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç session information track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Personalization:** Cookies ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ preferences (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: theme, language) save ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá website ‡¶ï‡ßá personalize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Tracking and Analytics:** Cookies ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user behavior ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç website ‡¶è‡¶∞ statistics track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Shopping Carts:** E-commerce websites ‡¶è cookies ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ shopping cart ‡¶è‡¶∞ items track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 3. How to Create, Read, and Delete Cookies

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá cookies create, read, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç delete ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø step ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

#### 3.1 Creating a Cookie

Cookies create ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `document.cookie` property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
document.cookie = "cookieName=cookieValue; expires=expirationDate; path=/";
```

- **cookieName:** Cookie ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡•§
- **cookieValue:** Cookie ‡¶è‡¶∞ value‡•§
- **expires (optional):** Cookie ‡¶è‡¶∞ expiration date‡•§
- **path (optional):** Cookie ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® path ‡¶è applicable ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
document.cookie =
  "username=JohnDoe; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 2024 12:00:00 UTC; path=/";
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `username` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø cookie ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ value ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã `JohnDoe` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø 2024 ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ 31 ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### 3.2 Reading a Cookie

Cookies read ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ì `document.cookie` property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨ cookies return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã current domain ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
console.log(document.cookie); // Outputs all cookies for the current domain
```

#### 3.3 Deleting a Cookie

Cookies delete ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø cookie ‡¶è‡¶∞ expiration date ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø past date ‡¶è set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
document.cookie =
  "cookieName=cookieValue; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 UTC; path=/";
```

##### Example:

```javascript
document.cookie = "username=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 UTC; path=/"; // Deletes the "username" cookie
```

**Explanation:** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `username` cookie ‡¶è‡¶∞ value empty ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç expiration date ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶§‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ cookie ‡¶ï‡ßá effectively delete ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### 4. Real-life Example of Using Cookies

#### Scenario: Storing and Retrieving User Preferences

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user "Dark Theme" ‡¶¨‡¶æ "Light Theme" select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ü‡¶ø cookie ‡¶§‡ßá save ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá page visit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á theme automatically apply ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### HTML + JavaScript + CSS Example:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>Theme Selector</title>
    <style>
      /* Basic styling for the body */
      body {
        font-family: Arial, sans-serif;
        transition: background-color 0.3s ease, color 0.3s ease;
      }

      /* Light theme styles */
      body.light {
        background-color: #f0f0f0;
        color: #333;
      }

      /* Dark theme styles */
      body.dark {
        background-color: #333;
        color: #f0f0f0;
      }

      /* Button styling */
      .theme-btn {
        margin: 20px;
        padding: 10px 20px;
        font-size: 16px;
        cursor: pointer;
        border: none;
        border-radius: 5px;
        transition: background-color 0.3s ease;
      }

      /* Light theme button */
      .theme-btn.light-btn {
        background-color: #fff;
        color: #333;
        box-shadow: 0 3px 6px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);
      }

      .theme-btn.light-btn:hover {
        background-color: #ddd;
      }

      /* Dark theme button */
      .theme-btn.dark-btn {
        background-color: #444;
        color: #fff;
        box-shadow: 0 3px 6px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
      }

      .theme-btn.dark-btn:hover {
        background-color: #222;
      }

      /* Styling for the theme choice section */
      .container {
        text-align: center;
        margin-top: 50px;
      }

      .container h1 {
        font-size: 2em;
        margin-bottom: 20px;
      }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <div class="container">
      <h1>Select Your Theme</h1>
      <button class="theme-btn light-btn" onclick="setTheme('light')">
        Light Theme
      </button>
      <button class="theme-btn dark-btn" onclick="setTheme('dark')">
        Dark Theme
      </button>
    </div>

    <script>
      // Function to set the theme and save it in a cookie
      function setTheme(theme) {
        document.cookie =
          "theme=" + theme + "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 2024 12:00:00 UTC; path=/";
        document.body.className = theme;
      }

      // Function to check the saved theme from cookies and apply it
      function applyThemeFromCookie() {
        let cookies = document.cookie.split("; ");
        for (let i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
          let cookie = cookies[i].split("=");
          if (cookie[0] === "theme") {
            document.body.className = cookie[1];
          }
        }
      }

      // Apply the theme when the page loads
      applyThemeFromCookie();
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
```

### Explanation:

1. **HTML Structure:**

   - ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø "Dark Theme" ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç "Light Theme" select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø button ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

2. **CSS Styling:**

   - **`body.light`**: Light theme ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø background ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç text color adjust ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
   - **`body.dark`**: Dark theme ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø dark background ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç light text color set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
   - Button ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶§‡ßá hover effects ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç smooth transition add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá look ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

3. **JavaScript:**
   - **`setTheme()`** function theme set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç cookie ‡¶§‡ßá save ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
   - **`applyThemeFromCookie()`** function cookie ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá theme ‡¶è‡¶∞ value check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ theme apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Screenshot:**
![cookie](./chapter-17/cookie.png)

**Code**
CodePen Link: https://codepen.io/FarmerAbdulAlim/pen/oNrmWKZ

### Result:

User ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® "Dark Theme" ‡¶¨‡¶æ "Light Theme" select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á theme apply ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç cookie ‡¶§‡ßá save ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶§‡ßá page ‡¶è revisit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá, saved theme automatically apply ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

### 5. Cookie Expiration and Path

Cookies ‡¶è‡¶∞ expiration date ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç path set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã cookies ‡¶è‡¶∞ lifespan ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç availability control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

- **Expiration Date:** Cookie ‡¶ï‡¶§‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ browser ‡¶è ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø expiration date set ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá cookie ‡¶ü‡¶ø session cookie ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç browser ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá expire ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

  ##### Example:

  ```javascript
  document.cookie =
    "username=JohnDoe; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 2024 12:00:00 UTC; path=/";
  ```

- **Path:** Cookie ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® path ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø applicable ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ By default, cookie ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá path ‡¶è set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á path ‡¶è accessible ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Cookie ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã domain ‡¶è accessible ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `path=/` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

  ##### Example:

  ```javascript
  document.cookie = "username=JohnDoe; path=/"; // Accessible on all pages within the domain
  ```

### 6. Conclusion

**JavaScript Cookies** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø powerful feature ‡¶Ø‡¶æ websites ‡¶ï‡ßá user-specific data store ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Cookies user ‡¶è‡¶∞ preferences, session management, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç tracking ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá cookies create, read, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç delete ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Proper expiration date ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç path set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá

cookies ‡¶ï‡ßá efficiently manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§ Cookies modern web development ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user experience ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡•§

### 1. Introduction to Web API

**Web API (Application Programming Interface)** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø interface ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá web applications ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Web API ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ request ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Web API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá external resources ‡¶¨‡¶æ services ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá interact ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: database, third-party services, cloud storage ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

#### Key Characteristics of Web API:

- API ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã HTTP/HTTPS ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- API ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ JSON ‡¶¨‡¶æ XML ‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡ßá data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Client-side ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá server-side ‡¶è communication ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 2. Why Use Web API?

Web API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

- **Data Sharing:** ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá data share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Third-party Integration:** External services (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: Google Maps, Payment Gateway) ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá integrate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Single Codebase with Multiple Clients:** API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø backend API ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã front-end application (‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤, ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á codebase ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá interact ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Interoperability:** ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® language ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç platforms ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data exchange ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 3. Types of Web APIs

Web API ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:

1. **REST (Representational State Transfer) APIs:** RESTful API ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã HTTP methods (GET, POST, PUT, DELETE) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá resources access ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç widely used API standard‡•§
2. **SOAP (Simple Object Access Protocol) APIs:** SOAP API ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã XML ‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡ßá message exchange ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø WSDL (Web Services Description Language) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá strict standards maintain ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### 4. Making API Requests

Web API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTTP request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ common HTTP request methods ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

#### 4.1 GET Request

**GET** method server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á request ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ API endpoints ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
fetch("https://api.example.com/data")
  .then((response) => response.json())
  .then((data) => console.log(data))
  .catch((error) => console.error("Error:", error));
```

**Explanation:**

- `fetch` function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø GET request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Response data JSON ‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡ßá parse ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá console ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### 4.2 POST Request

**POST** method server ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® data create ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
fetch("https://api.example.com/data", {
  method: "POST",
  headers: {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
  },
  body: JSON.stringify({
    name: "John Doe",
    email: "johndoe@example.com",
  }),
})
  .then((response) => response.json())
  .then((data) => console.log("Success:", data))
  .catch((error) => console.error("Error:", error));
```

**Explanation:**

- ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø POST request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user data (name, email) ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Request body JSON ‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç response success message return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### 4.3 PUT and DELETE Requests

**PUT** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **DELETE** requests server ‡¶è data update ‡¶¨‡¶æ delete ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### PUT Example (Update):

```javascript
fetch("https://api.example.com/data/1", {
  method: "PUT",
  headers: {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
  },
  body: JSON.stringify({
    name: "Jane Doe",
    email: "janedoe@example.com",
  }),
})
  .then((response) => response.json())
  .then((data) => console.log("Updated:", data))
  .catch((error) => console.error("Error:", error));
```

##### DELETE Example (Delete):

```javascript
fetch("https://api.example.com/data/1", {
  method: "DELETE",
})
  .then((response) => response.json())
  .then((data) => console.log("Deleted:", data))
  .catch((error) => console.error("Error:", error));
```

### 5. Real-life Example of Using Web API

#### Scenario: Fetching Weather Data from a Public API

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø weather API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **OpenWeatherMap API** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>Weather App</title>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>Current Weather</h1>
    <div id="weather"></div>

    <script>
      const apiKey = "your_api_key_here";
      const city = "Dhaka";
      const apiUrl = `https://api.openweathermap.org/data/2.5/weather?q=${city}&appid=${apiKey}`;

      fetch(apiUrl)
        .then((response) => response.json())
        .then((data) => {
          const weatherDiv = document.getElementById("weather");
          const temp = data.main.temp - 273.15; // Convert from Kelvin to Celsius
          weatherDiv.innerHTML = `<h2>${city}</h2><p>Temperature: ${temp.toFixed(
            2
          )}¬∞C</p>`;
        })
        .catch((error) => console.error("Error fetching weather data:", error));
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
```

**Explanation:**

- ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **OpenWeatherMap API** ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¢‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡¶π‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `fetch` function ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá API call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç response data ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 6. Handling API Responses

API response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:

1. **Response Status Check:** ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá, response status check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, success (200) ‡¶¨‡¶æ error response ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
2. **Parsing the Response:** Response data ‡¶ï‡ßá JSON ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø format ‡¶è parse ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Displaying Data:** Parsed data ‡¶ï‡ßá UI ‡¶§‡ßá display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
fetch("https://api.example.com/data")
  .then((response) => {
    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error("Network response was not ok");
    }
    return response.json();
  })
  .then((data) => console.log(data))
  .catch((error) =>
    console.error("There was a problem with the fetch operation:", error)
  );
```

**Explanation:**

- ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá response status check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø response "ok" ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá error throw ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- Response JSON ‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡ßá parse ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 7. Error Handling in API Requests

Error handling ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ API requests ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶á, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ network issues ‡¶¨‡¶æ server errors ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Error handling ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `try-catch` block ‡¶¨‡¶æ `.catch()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
fetch("https://api.example.com/data")
  .then((response) => {
    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error("Failed to fetch data");
    }
    return response.json();
  })
  .then((data) => console.log(data))
  .catch((error) => {
    console.error("Error occurred:", error.message);
  });
```

**Explanation:**

- ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø API call ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã error ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá `.catch()` block ‡¶è error handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- Error message console ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

### 1. Introduction to Constraint Validation API

**Constraint Validation API** HTML5 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø powerful feature, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ form elements validation ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á API automatically certain conditions validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: required fields, input types, maximum ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç minimum values), ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá form validation process ‡¶ï‡ßá programmatically manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Key Features:

- **HTML form validation** client-side ‡¶è validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Custom validation rules apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá form validation behavior override ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Built-in validation methods ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç properties ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã advanced validation ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Source: [W3Schools - JavaScript Validation API](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_validation_api.asp)

---

### 2. Why Use Constraint Validation API?

**Constraint Validation API** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

1. **Built-in Validation:** HTML form elements ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `<input>`, `<textarea>`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `<select>` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø automatic validation ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Custom Validation Messages:** Default error messages ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá custom error messages define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Programmatic Validation:** JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá manual validation control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
4. **Client-side Validation:** Server-side validation ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶á client-side validation ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ mistakes early detect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user experience ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 3. Basic DOM Methods for Validation

HTML form elements validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Constraint Validation API ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ DOM methods ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 3.1 checkValidity()

**`checkValidity()`** method form element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá true ‡¶¨‡¶æ false return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, depending on whether the element meets all its validation constraints.

##### Syntax:

```javascript
element.checkValidity();
```

##### Example:

```html
<form id="myForm">
  <input type="text" id="username" required />
  <div id="error-message"></div>
  <!-- Error message will be displayed here -->
  <button type="submit" onclick="validateForm(event)">Submit</button>
</form>

<script>
  function validateForm(event) {
    const input = document.getElementById("username");
    const errorMessage = document.getElementById("error-message");

    if (!input.checkValidity()) {
      errorMessage.textContent = "Please fill out the required field."; // Output to the div
      event.preventDefault(); // Prevent form submission
    } else {
      errorMessage.textContent = ""; // Clear error if valid
    }
  }
</script>
```

**Explanation:**

- **`checkValidity()`** method check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `username` field valid ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- Output alert message ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML element (div) ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `username` field empty ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá "Please fill out the required field." div ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### 3.2 setCustomValidity()

**`setCustomValidity()`** method element ‡¶è‡¶∞ default validation message override ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá custom error message set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
element.setCustomValidity(message);
```

##### Example:

```html
<form id="myForm">
  <input type="text" id="username" required />
  <div id="error-message"></div>
  <!-- Error message will be displayed here -->
  <button type="submit" onclick="validateCustomMessage(event)">Submit</button>
</form>

<script>
  function validateCustomMessage(event) {
    const input = document.getElementById("username");
    const errorMessage = document.getElementById("error-message");

    if (input.value === "") {
      input.setCustomValidity("Username is required!");
      errorMessage.textContent = input.validationMessage; // Show error message in div
      event.preventDefault(); // Prevent form submission
    } else {
      input.setCustomValidity(""); // Clear custom message when valid
      errorMessage.textContent = ""; // Clear error message
    }
  }
</script>
```

**Explanation:**

- **`setCustomValidity()`** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá custom validation message set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Validation message HTML element (div) ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá custom error message "Username is required!" ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### 4. Validation Properties

Constraint Validation API ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ properties ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ form elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ validation state ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 4.1 validity

**`validity`** property ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø object return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ element ‡¶è‡¶∞ validation state ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá boolean values ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
const input = document.getElementById("username");
if (input.validity.valueMissing) {
  document.getElementById("error-message").textContent =
    "This field is required.";
}
```

#### 4.2 validationMessage

**`validationMessage`** property element ‡¶è‡¶∞ current validation error message return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø element valid ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø empty string return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
const input = document.getElementById("username");
document.getElementById("error-message").textContent = input.validationMessage;
```

#### 4.3 willValidate

**`willValidate`** property true ‡¶¨‡¶æ false return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, depending on whether the element is subject to validation.

##### Example:

```javascript
const input = document.getElementById("username");
console.log(input.willValidate); // true if the input is subject to validation
```

---

### 5. Real-life Example of Form Validation

#### Scenario: Registration Form Validation

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø registration form ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá username ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç password field ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç form submit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá validation check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>Registration Form</title>
  </head>
  <body>
    <form id="registrationForm">
      <label for="username">Username:</label>
      <input type="text" id="username" required minlength="5" />
      <div id="username-error"></div>
      <!-- Username error message here -->

      <label for="password">Password:</label>
      <input type="password" id="password" required minlength="8" />
      <div id="password-error"></div>
      <!-- Password error message here -->

      <button type="submit" onclick="validateRegistrationForm(event)">
        Register
      </button>
    </form>

    <script>
      function validateRegistrationForm(event) {
        const username = document.getElementById("username");
        const password = document.getElementById("password");
        const usernameError = document.getElementById("username-error");
        const passwordError = document.getElementById("password-error");

        // Username validation
        if (!username.checkValidity()) {
          usernameError.textContent = username.validationMessage;
          event.preventDefault(); // Prevent form submission
        } else {
          usernameError.textContent = ""; // Clear error message if valid
        }

        // Password validation
        if (!password.checkValidity()) {
          passwordError.textContent = password.validationMessage;
          event.preventDefault(); // Prevent form submission
        } else {
          passwordError.textContent = ""; // Clear error message if valid
        }
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
```

**Explanation:**

- `username` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `password` fields ‡¶è‡¶∞ validation message ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø `<div>` element ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Output:
  - ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `username` 5 characters ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá "Please lengthen this text to 5 characters or more." ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
  - ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `password` 8 characters ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá "Please lengthen this text to 8 characters or more." ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### 6. Customizing Error Messages

HTML form validation ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ built-in error messages ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`setCustomValidity()`** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá custom error messages define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
const password = document.getElementById("password");
const passwordError = document.getElementById("password-error");

password.oninput = function () {
  if (password.value.length < 8) {
    password.setCustomValidity("Password must be at least 8 characters long.");
    passwordError.textContent = password.validationMessage; // Display custom message
  } else {
    password.setCustomValidity(""); // Clear custom message if valid
    passwordError.textContent = ""; // Clear error message
  }
};
```

---

### 7. Validity Properties Table

HTML form elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ validity state ‡¶ï‡ßá track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® properties ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ boolean values return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ Table ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Validity Properties ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

| Property | Description |
| -------- | ----------- |

|
| `valid` | Field valid ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ True ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá field valid, false ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá invalid‡•§ |
| `valueMissing` | Field required ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç empty ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
| `typeMismatch` | Input type ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: email ‡¶¨‡¶æ URL ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá mismatch ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ |
| `patternMismatch`| Field ‡¶è‡¶∞ value ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø pattern attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá mismatch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ |
| `tooLong` | Input ‡¶è‡¶∞ value ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø maxlength attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ limit ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ |
| `tooShort` | Input ‡¶è‡¶∞ value ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø minlength attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ limit ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ |
| `rangeUnderflow` | Input ‡¶è‡¶∞ value ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø min attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ limit ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ |
| `rangeOverflow` | Input ‡¶è‡¶∞ value ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø max attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ limit ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ |
| `stepMismatch` | Input ‡¶è‡¶∞ value ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø step attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá mismatch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ |
| `badInput` | Input ‡¶è‡¶∞ value ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø number ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ |
| `customError` | Custom validation message set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ |

---

### 8. Conclusion

**Constraint Validation API** form validation ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç customizable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á API ‡¶è‡¶∞ built-in methods ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç properties ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá HTML form validation automatic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JavaScript ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá custom validation messages ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç rules ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Validation messages HTML element ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá user experience ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá form validation process ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

### 1. Introduction to Web Storage API

**Web Storage API** HTML5 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø feature, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ client-side data storage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Web Storage API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá browser ‡¶è data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ cookies ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø data ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø faster ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø secure‡•§

#### Key Features:

- Web Storage data ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ client-side ‡¶è store ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, server-side ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- Two types of storage: **Local Storage** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Session Storage**‡•§
- Cookies ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø storage capacity (‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º 5-10MB)‡•§

Source: [W3Schools - Web Storage API](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_api_web_storage.asp)

---

### 2. Why Use Web Storage API?

**Web Storage API** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

1. **Increased Storage Capacity:** Cookies ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º web storage ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá (‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º 5-10MB)‡•§
2. **Faster and More Secure:** Cookies ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá server ‡¶è data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç security risks ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡•§
3. **Persistent and Session-based Storage:** Web Storage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá data session-based ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ long-term store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
4. **Simple API:** Web Storage API ‡¶è‡¶∞ methods ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÄ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 3. Types of Web Storage

Web Storage API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ storage ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º: **Local Storage** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Session Storage**‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, **Local Storage** data ‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø store ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **Session Storage** data ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ session ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ store ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

#### 3.1 Local Storage

**Local Storage** data persistent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé browser close ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì data remove ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø long-term storage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
// Local Storage ‡¶è data set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
localStorage.setItem("username", "JohnDoe");

// Local Storage ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data get ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
let user = localStorage.getItem("username");
console.log(user); // Output: JohnDoe
```

#### 3.2 Session Storage

**Session Storage** data ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ session (‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ browser window/tab open ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Browser ‡¶¨‡¶æ tab close ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá data remove ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
// Session Storage ‡¶è data set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
sessionStorage.setItem("username", "JaneDoe");

// Session Storage ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data get ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
let user = sessionStorage.getItem("username");
console.log(user); // Output: JaneDoe
```

---

### 4. Basic Methods of Web Storage

Web Storage API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá data store, retrieve, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Web Storage API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ methods ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

#### 4.1 setItem()

**`setItem()`** method Web Storage ‡¶è data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø key-value pair ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
storage.setItem(key, value);
```

##### Example:

```javascript
localStorage.setItem("username", "JohnDoe"); // Local Storage ‡¶è data set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
```

#### 4.2 getItem()

**`getItem()`** method Web Storage ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
storage.getItem(key);
```

##### Example:

```javascript
let user = localStorage.getItem("username"); // Local Storage ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data get ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
console.log(user); // Output: JohnDoe
```

#### 4.3 removeItem()

**`removeItem()`** method Web Storage ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü data remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
storage.removeItem(key);
```

##### Example:

```javascript
localStorage.removeItem("username"); // Local Storage ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 'username' remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
```

#### 4.4 clear()

**`clear()`** method Web Storage ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ data remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
storage.clear();
```

##### Example:

```javascript
localStorage.clear(); // Local Storage ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ data remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
```

---

### 5. Real-life Example of Using Web Storage API

#### Scenario: Simple Theme Toggle using Local Storage

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø webpage ‡¶è dark mode ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç light mode ‡¶è‡¶∞ theme toggle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á theme preference ‡¶ï‡ßá **Local Storage** ‡¶è store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá user ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® page reload ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶§‡ßá visit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á preference restore ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>Theme Toggle</title>
    <style>
      body {
        font-family: Arial, sans-serif;
        background-color: white;
        color: black;
      }
      body.dark-mode {
        background-color: black;
        color: white;
      }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>Theme Toggle with Web Storage</h1>
    <button onclick="toggleTheme()">Toggle Theme</button>

    <script>
      // Function to toggle theme
      function toggleTheme() {
        const body = document.body;
        body.classList.toggle("dark-mode");

        // Store the user's preference in Local Storage
        if (body.classList.contains("dark-mode")) {
          localStorage.setItem("theme", "dark");
        } else {
          localStorage.setItem("theme", "light");
        }
      }

      // Load user's theme preference from Local Storage
      window.onload = function () {
        const theme = localStorage.getItem("theme");
        if (theme === "dark") {
          document.body.classList.add("dark-mode");
        }
      };
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
```

**Explanation:**

- Theme toggle ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø button ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **dark mode** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **light mode** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá toggle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Local Storage** ‡¶è theme preference store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá user reload ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì preference save ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

---

### 6. Storage Object Properties and Methods

Web Storage API ‡¶è‡¶∞ Storage object ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ data store, retrieve, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods ‡¶è‡¶∞ table ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

| Property/Method       | Description                                                   |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `setItem(key, value)` | Web Storage ‡¶è key-value pair ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§           |
| `getItem(key)`        | Web Storage ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü key ‡¶è‡¶∞ value return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§           |
| `removeItem(key)`     | Web Storage ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü key ‡¶è‡¶∞ data remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§            |
| `clear()`             | Web Storage ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ data remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§                       |
| `key(index)`          | Web Storage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü index ‡¶è ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ key return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§         |
| `length`              | Web Storage ‡¶è ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ total key-value pair ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |

##### Example of `key(index)` and `length`:

```javascript
// Set two items in Local Storage
localStorage.setItem("username", "JohnDoe");
localStorage.setItem("email", "john@example.com");

// Get the key at index 1
let key = localStorage.key(1);
console.log(key); // Output: 'email'

// Get the total number of items in Local Storage
let length = localStorage.length;
console.log(length); // Output: 2
```

---

### 7. Limitations of Web Storage

Web Storage API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡ßÄ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

1. **Limited Storage Capacity:** Local ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Session Storage ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º 5-10MB ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
2. **No Server-Side Interaction:** Web Storage server-side ‡¶è accessible ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá data sharing ‡¶¨‡¶æ synchronization ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
3. **Same-Origin Policy:** Web Storage ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á origin (domain, protocol, port) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Cross-origin ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
4. **Security:** Sensitive information ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® passwords Web Storage ‡¶è store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá easily accessible‡•§

---

### 8. Conclusion

**Web Storage API** HTML5 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ feature, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ client-side ‡¶è data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø cookies ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø storage capacity ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Web Storage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã: **Local Storage** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Session Storage**‡•§ Local Storage ‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Session Storage session ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá data store ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç

retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

### 1. Introduction to Web Workers API

**Web Workers API** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø JavaScript API, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ background ‡¶è JavaScript ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá main UI thread ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá‡•§ Web Workers API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá complex ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç time-consuming tasks background ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶É calculations ‡¶¨‡¶æ data processing, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### Key Features:

- JavaScript code background ‡¶è run ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá UI responsive ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
- Web Workers API ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø separate file ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç main thread ‡¶ï‡ßá block ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- Workers cannot directly manipulate the DOM.

Source: [W3Schools - Web Workers API](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_api_web_workers.asp)

---

### 2. Why Use Web Workers API?

**Web Workers API** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

1. **Asynchronous Processing:** Web Workers background ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, main UI thread block ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Performance Improvement:** Complex ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç heavy computation tasks background ‡¶è run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá page freeze ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user experience ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Separate Execution Context:** Web Workers ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨ execution context ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø directly DOM access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ security ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
4. **Multithreading Support in JavaScript:** JavaScript ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ single-threaded, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Web Workers API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ JavaScript ‡¶è pseudo-multithreading ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

---

### 3. Creating a Web Worker

Web Worker ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ worker script ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø separate JavaScript file ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç main thread ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **`new Worker()`** constructor ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø instantiate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### Example:

```javascript
// worker.js (Web Worker Script)
onmessage = function (e) {
  let result = e.data * 2; // Double the input
  postMessage(result); // Send the result back to the main script
};
```

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>Web Workers Example</title>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>Web Workers Demo</h1>
    <button onclick="startWorker()">Start Worker</button>
    <p>Result: <span id="result"></span></p>

    <script>
      let worker;

      function startWorker() {
        if (typeof Worker !== "undefined") {
          if (!worker) {
            worker = new Worker("worker.js"); // Create a new Web Worker
          }

          worker.postMessage(10); // Send data to Web Worker

          worker.onmessage = function (e) {
            document.getElementById("result").textContent = e.data; // Display result
          };
        } else {
          document.getElementById("result").textContent =
            "Web Workers are not supported in your browser.";
        }
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
```

**Explanation:**

- `worker.js` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Web Worker script, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá main script ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá calculation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Main script ‡¶è `new Worker()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá worker create ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Web Worker ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá result main thread ‡¶è ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶§ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 4. Web Worker Methods

Web Workers API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá main script ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç worker ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data exchange ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 4.1 postMessage()

**`postMessage()`** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá main script ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Web Worker ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Web Worker ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá main script ‡¶è data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
worker.postMessage(data);
```

##### Example:

```javascript
worker.postMessage("Hello, Worker!"); // Main script ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Web Worker ‡¶è message ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã
```

#### 4.2 terminate()

**`terminate()`** method Web Worker ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø worker ‡¶ï‡ßá immediately terminate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
worker.terminate();
```

##### Example:

```javascript
worker.terminate(); // Web Worker ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
```

---

### 5. Communicating with Web Workers

Main script ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Web Worker ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá communication **message events** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Web Worker ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º **`postMessage()`** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Web Worker ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá main script ‡¶è data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Main Script ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Web Worker ‡¶è Message ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã:

```javascript
worker.postMessage("Some data"); // Data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã
```

##### Web Worker ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Main Script ‡¶è Message ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã:

```javascript
postMessage(result); // Web Worker ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá main script ‡¶è result ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã
```

##### Main Script ‡¶è Message Receive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ:

```javascript
worker.onmessage = function (e) {
  console.log("Message from Worker:", e.data);
};
```

##### Web Worker ‡¶è Message Receive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ:

```javascript
onmessage = function (e) {
  console.log("Message from Main Script:", e.data);
};
```

---

### 6. Real-life Example of Using Web Workers API

#### Scenario: Performing a Large Calculation in the Background

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® factorial) calculate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Web Worker ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á calculation background ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
// worker.js (Web Worker Script)
onmessage = function (e) {
  let num = e.data;
  let result = 1;
  for (let i = num; i > 1; i--) {
    result *= i;
  }
  postMessage(result); // Result back to the main script
};
```

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>Factorial Calculation with Web Workers</title>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>Calculate Factorial using Web Workers</h1>
    <button onclick="startWorker()">Calculate Factorial of 10</button>
    <p>Result: <span id="result"></span></p>

    <script>
      let worker;

      function startWorker() {
        if (typeof Worker !== "undefined") {
          if (!worker) {
            worker = new Worker("worker.js"); // Create a new Web Worker
          }

          worker.postMessage(10); // Send number to Web Worker for factorial calculation

          worker.onmessage = function (e) {
            document.getElementById("result").textContent = e.data; // Display result
          };
        } else {
          document.getElementById("result").textContent =
            "Web Workers are not supported in your browser.";
        }
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
```

**Explanation:**

- `worker.js` file ‡¶è factorial calculate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Main thread ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **Web Worker** ‡¶è 10 ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç calculation ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá result HTML page ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 7. Limitations of Web Workers

Web Workers API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡ßÄ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

1. **No DOM Access:** Web Workers DOM access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø main UI thread ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá completely separate‡•§
2. **Same-Origin Policy:** Web Workers ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á origin (domain, protocol, port) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Cross-origin workers create ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
3. **Limited to File-based Execution:** Web Workers ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ file ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, inline worker script ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
4. **Resource-Intensive:** Web Workers background ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì, ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ workers create ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ resource-intensive ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 8. Conclusion

**Web Workers API** ‡¶π‡¶≤ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ feature, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ background ‡¶è tasks run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá page ‡¶è‡¶∞ responsiveness ‡¶¨‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø asynchronous ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç parallel execution ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ complex ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç heavy tasks background ‡¶è run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡ßÄ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø essential tool, ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® performance optimization ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user experience ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
