### 1. Introduction to Fetch API

**Fetch API** ‡¶π‡¶≤ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø built-in interface, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ asynchronous HTTP requests ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Fetch API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ external resources (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶É API, servers) ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø modern browsers ‡¶è available ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç XMLHttpRequest (XHR) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ Fetch API ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible‡•§

#### Key Features:

- Fetch API asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Promise-based‡•§
- Fetch API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø HTTP requests ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Fetch API responses ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ JSON format ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø data formats (text, blob) ‡¶ì handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Source: [W3Schools - Fetch API](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_api_fetch.asp)

---

### 2. Why Use Fetch API?

**Fetch API** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

1. **Asynchronous Requests:** Fetch API asynchronous requests handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ UI responsive ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
2. **Promise-based:** Fetch API promise-based ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, request ‡¶è‡¶∞ result chainable, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `.then()` ‡¶ì `.catch()` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá errors handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Simpler Syntax:** Fetch API ‡¶è‡¶∞ syntax XHR ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç concise‡•§
4. **More Powerful:** Fetch API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá request headers, credentials, response handling, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç CORS support ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 3. Basic Syntax of Fetch API

Fetch API ‡¶è‡¶∞ basic syntax ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

```javascript
fetch(url)
  .then((response) => {
    // Handle the response
  })
  .catch((error) => {
    // Handle any errors
  });
```

- **`fetch(url)`**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `url` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã resource ‡¶è‡¶∞ URL ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- Fetch API ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **promise** return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `.then()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
- `.catch()` block ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá request ‡¶è‡¶∞ errors handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 4. Making GET Requests

#### Using Promise

##### Example:

```javascript
fetch("https://api.example.com/data")
  .then((response) => response.json()) // Parse the response as JSON
  .then((data) => console.log(data)) // Handle the JSON data
  .catch((error) => console.error("Error:", error)); // Handle any errors
```

#### Using Async/Await for GET Request

Async/Await ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á GET request ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
async function fetchData() {
  try {
    const response = await fetch("https://api.example.com/data"); // Send the GET request
    const data = await response.json(); // Parse the JSON response
    console.log(data); // Handle the data
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Error:", error); // Handle any errors
  }
}

fetchData(); // Call the async function
```

**Explanation:**

- `async/await` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá asynchronous GET request ‡¶ï‡ßá synchronous ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ code ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì readable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
- `await` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá response ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 5. Making POST Requests

#### Using Promise for POST

##### Example:

```javascript
fetch("https://api.example.com/data", {
  method: "POST",
  headers: {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
  },
  body: JSON.stringify({
    name: "John Doe",
    email: "john.doe@example.com",
  }),
})
  .then((response) => response.json())
  .then((data) => console.log("Success:", data))
  .catch((error) => console.error("Error:", error));
```

#### Using Async/Await for POST Request

##### Example:

```javascript
async function postData() {
  try {
    const response = await fetch("https://api.example.com/data", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        name: "John Doe",
        email: "john.doe@example.com",
      }),
    });
    const data = await response.json(); // Parse the JSON response
    console.log("Success:", data); // Handle the data
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Error:", error); // Handle any errors
  }
}

postData(); // Call the async function
```

**Explanation:**

- Async/Await ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá POST request handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `await` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá response ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 6. Handling Responses

Fetch API responses ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ status ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá‡•§ Response ‡¶è‡¶∞ status ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `.then()` block ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
fetch("https://api.example.com/data")
  .then((response) => {
    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error("Network response was not ok");
    }
    return response.json(); // Parse response if successful
  })
  .then((data) => console.log(data))
  .catch((error) =>
    console.error("There was a problem with the fetch operation:", error)
  );
```

**Explanation:**

- `response.ok` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá response ‡¶è‡¶∞ status check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø response status `200` ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá error throw ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Response JSON format ‡¶è parse ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `.catch()` block ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá error handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 7. Real-life Example of Using Fetch API

#### With Button Click

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶¨ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **button click** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá API ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç HTML ‡¶è display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>Fetch API Example</title>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>Users</h1>
    <button onclick="fetchUserData()">Load Users</button>
    <ul id="userList"></ul>

    <script>
      // Async function to fetch user data
      async function fetchUserData() {
        try {
          const response = await fetch(
            "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users"
          ); // Fetch data
          const data = await response.json(); // Parse JSON response
          const userList = document.getElementById("userList");

          // Loop through the data and display users in the list
          data.forEach((user) => {
            const listItem = document.createElement("li");
            listItem.textContent = `${user.name} - ${user.email}`;
            userList.appendChild(listItem);
          });
        } catch (error) {
          console.error("Error fetching user data:", error); // Handle errors
        }
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
```

**Explanation:**

- User data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Load Users** button ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá `fetchUserData()` function call ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **Async/Await** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Fetched data HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ `<ul>` element ‡¶è dynamically add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 8. Handling Errors in Fetch API

Error handling Fetch API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡•§ Fetch API errors handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `.catch()` block ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Common errors ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã network issues ‡¶¨‡¶æ invalid responses‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
fetch("https://api.example.com/invalid-url")
  .then((response) => {
    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
    }
    return response.json();
  })
  .then((data) => console.log(data))
  .catch((error) => console.error("Fetch error:", error));
```

**Explanation:**

- Invalid URL ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá error throw ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `response.ok` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá response status check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `.catch()` block ‡¶è error message ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 9. Conclusion

**Fetch API** ‡¶π‡¶≤ modern JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible interface, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ asynchronous HTTP requests ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç responses handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø promise-based ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ GET, POST, PUT, DELETE ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã HTTP requests handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Async/Await ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Fetch API ‡¶è‡¶∞ code ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì readable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç cleaner ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Fetch API responses ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ JSON format ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `.then()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `.catch()`

‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ response ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç errors handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá complex API requests ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

### 1. Introduction to Geolocation API

**Geolocation API** ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø JavaScript API, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® (longitude ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç latitude) ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá device ‡¶è‡¶∞ location tracking ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§ Geolocation API web applications ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá personalized content ‡¶¨‡¶æ services ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Key Features:

- Geolocation API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ actual ‡¶¨‡¶æ estimated physical location ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- API asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user ‡¶è‡¶∞ permission ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Geolocation API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® method ‡¶π‡¶≤ **`getCurrentPosition()`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`watchPosition()`**‡•§

Source: [W3Schools - Geolocation API](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_api_geolocation.asp)

---

### 2. Why Use Geolocation API?

**Geolocation API** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

1. **Personalized User Experience:** Geolocation API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá location-based personalized services ‡¶¨‡¶æ content ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **Real-time Tracking:** **watchPosition()** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ real-time location track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Map-based Services:** Geolocation API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá web applications ‡¶è map-based services integrate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: Google Maps‡•§
4. **Asynchronous Execution:** API asynchronous ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º page ‡¶è‡¶∞ performance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

---

### 3. Basic Syntax of Geolocation API

Geolocation API ‡¶è‡¶∞ basic syntax ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

```javascript
navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(successCallback, errorCallback);
```

- **`getCurrentPosition()`**: ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø asynchronous ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø success ‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø error callback function ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§
- **`successCallback`**: ‡¶è‡¶á function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá successful position data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **`errorCallback`**: ‡¶è‡¶á function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã error ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 4. Getting the User's Location

#### Using getCurrentPosition()

**`getCurrentPosition()`** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ current position ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶á position return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
  function (position) {
    console.log("Latitude:", position.coords.latitude);
    console.log("Longitude:", position.coords.longitude);
  },
  function (error) {
    console.error("Error:", error.message);
  }
);
```

**Explanation:**

- `getCurrentPosition()` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ current latitude ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç longitude ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Success callback function ‡¶è position data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç console ‡¶è output ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Error callback function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã error ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

#### Using watchPosition()

**`watchPosition()`** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ location real-time ‡¶è track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø repeated updates ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶æ user ‡¶è‡¶∞ position ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
navigator.geolocation.watchPosition(
  function (position) {
    console.log("Latitude:", position.coords.latitude);
    console.log("Longitude:", position.coords.longitude);
  },
  function (error) {
    console.error("Error:", error.message);
  }
);
```

**Explanation:**

- `watchPosition()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ position updates ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- User ‡¶è‡¶∞ location ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® latitude ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç longitude console ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 5. Handling Geolocation Errors

Geolocation API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá errors ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: user permission deny ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, position unavailable, ‡¶¨‡¶æ request timeout‡•§ Geolocation API errors handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `errorCallback` function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá common errors ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ error code ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

| Error Code | Error Message        |
| ---------- | -------------------- |
| 1          | Permission denied    |
| 2          | Position unavailable |
| 3          | Timeout              |

##### Example:

```javascript
function errorCallback(error) {
  switch (error.code) {
    case error.PERMISSION_DENIED:
      console.error("User denied the request for Geolocation.");
      break;
    case error.POSITION_UNAVAILABLE:
      console.error("Location information is unavailable.");
      break;
    case error.TIMEOUT:
      console.error("The request to get user location timed out.");
      break;
    default:
      console.error("An unknown error occurred.");
      break;
  }
}

navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(successCallback, errorCallback);
```

---

### 6. Real-life Example of Using Geolocation API

#### With Button Click

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶¨ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ location fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá HTML ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>Geolocation API Example</title>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>Find My Location</h1>
    <button onclick="getLocation()">Get Location</button>
    <p id="location"></p>

    <script>
      // Function to get the user's location
      function getLocation() {
        const locationDisplay = document.getElementById("location");

        if (navigator.geolocation) {
          navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
            function (position) {
              const latitude = position.coords.latitude;
              const longitude = position.coords.longitude;
              locationDisplay.textContent = `Latitude: ${latitude}, Longitude: ${longitude}`;
            },
            function (error) {
              locationDisplay.textContent = `Error: ${error.message}`;
            }
          );
        } else {
          locationDisplay.textContent =
            "Geolocation is not supported by this browser.";
        }
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
```

**Explanation:**

- Button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá **getLocation()** function call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Geolocation API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ location fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Fetched location data HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ `<p>` element ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Geolocation API supported ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã error ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá error message ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 7. Limitations and Privacy Concerns

#### Limitations:

1. **User Permission Required:** Geolocation API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø user permission deny ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá location access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
2. **Accuracy Varies:** Device ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá location accuracy ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ GPS enabled devices ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø accurate data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Network Dependency:** Geolocation API ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá network ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤, ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá WiFi ‡¶¨‡¶æ mobile data connection ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### Privacy Concerns:

1. **Sensitive Data:** Geolocation data ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ sensitive, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á informed consent ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
2. **Data Misuse:** Web applications ‡¶è Geolocation data misused ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶• security measures ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Location Tracking:** Web applications ‡¶è continuous location tracking ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ privacy ‡¶π‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 8. Conclusion

**Geolocation API** ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ tool, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ actual ‡¶¨‡¶æ estimated physical location ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® location-based services ‡¶¨‡¶æ applications ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: weather apps, map-based services ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ Geolocation API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø method ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã `getCurrentPosition()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `watchPosition()`‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ privacy ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç security ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

### 1. Introduction to AJAX

**AJAX** (Asynchronous JavaScript and XML) ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø technology, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá web pages asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá data exchange ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ AJAX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá page reload ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá dynamically content load ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ XMLHttpRequest object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá AJAX ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá modern Fetch API ‡¶ì AJAX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Key Features:

- AJAX asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø content unaffected ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø page reload ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá dynamically content update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Data format ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá XML, JSON, HTML, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç plain text ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 2. Why Use AJAX?

AJAX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá web applications ‡¶è‡¶∞ responsiveness ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

1. **Asynchronous Data Loading:** AJAX asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá data fetch ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Improved User Experience:** Page reload ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá specific data fetch ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá user experience ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Efficient Data Requests:** AJAX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü data chunks server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá request ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ bandwidth ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
4. **Seamless Server Interactions:** AJAX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá GET, POST, PUT, DELETE ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø HTTP methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 3. How AJAX Works

AJAX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **client-side** ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **server-side** ‡¶è request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç response ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡ßá‡•§ AJAX ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ **XMLHttpRequest (XHR)** object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá AJAX ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

1. **Create an XMLHttpRequest Object:** AJAX request ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø `XMLHttpRequest` object ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
2. **Open a Request:** XMLHttpRequest ‡¶è‡¶∞ `.open()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá HTTP request ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
3. **Send the Request:** `.send()` method ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá request server ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
4. **Handle the Response:** Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá response data ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 4. Making AJAX Requests

#### GET Request

**GET** method server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø GET request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

##### Example:

```javascript
let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();

xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
  if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
    document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = this.responseText;
  }
};

xhttp.open("GET", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts/1", true);
xhttp.send();
```

- **Explanation:**
  - **open("GET", url, true):** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `"GET"` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `url` ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá server ‡¶è‡¶∞ API endpoint ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  - **onreadystatechange:** Request ‡¶è‡¶∞ state change ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á function execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® request ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® readyState ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç status check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
  - **this.readyState == 4:** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá request ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  - **this.status == 200:** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá request ‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ **status == 200** ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá successful HTTP request‡•§
  - **this.responseText:** Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response data HTML element ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### POST Request

**POST** method server ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ POST request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá server ‡¶è data create ‡¶¨‡¶æ update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();

xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
  if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 201) {
    document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = this.responseText;
  }
};

xhttp.open("POST", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts", true);
xhttp.setRequestHeader("Content-type", "application/json");

xhttp.send(
  JSON.stringify({
    title: "foo",
    body: "bar",
    userId: 1,
  })
);
```

- **Explanation:**
  - **open("POST", url, true):** POST request ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  - **setRequestHeader():** Content-type set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá server ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá JSON format ‡¶è data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  - **send():** JSON format ‡¶è serialized data server ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **JSON.stringify()** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá JavaScript object ‡¶ï‡ßá JSON format ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### Detailed Explanation of `xhttp.send(JSON.stringify({ title: "foo", body: "bar", userId: 1 }))`:

- **xhttp.send()**: ‡¶è‡¶á method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá XMLHttpRequest object request send ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **JSON.stringify()**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø JavaScript function ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript object ‡¶ï‡ßá JSON string ‡¶è convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ POST request ‡¶è server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡ßá data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, data ‡¶ï‡ßá JSON format ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `JSON.stringify()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§
- **Object Details**:
  - **title: "foo"**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `title` property ‡¶§‡ßá `"foo"` string ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  - **body: "bar"**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `body` property ‡¶§‡ßá `"bar"` string ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  - **userId: 1**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `userId` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ (number) ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- **Conclusion**: `send()` method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á serialized JSON data server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç server ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á data receive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

- **status == 201:** HTTP status code **201** ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá data ‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 5. Handling AJAX Responses

AJAX request ‡¶è‡¶∞ response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá, response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `onreadystatechange` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `onload` property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Using onreadystatechange

**onreadystatechange** property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® state track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç response data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ flexible ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç traditional approach‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
  if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
    document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = this.responseText;
  }
};
```

- **Explanation:**
  - Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ `readyState == 4` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `status == 200` check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá data HTML element ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### Using onload

**onload** property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá request ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `onreadystatechange` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç cleaner approach‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
xhttp.onload = function () {
  if (this.status == 200) {
    document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = this.responseText;
  }
};
```

- **Explanation:**
  - Request ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá **onload** execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç request ‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá response data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá HTML element ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 6. Real-life Example of AJAX

#### With Button Click

‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá AJAX request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç HTML element ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>AJAX Example</title>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>AJAX Demo</h1>
    <button onclick="loadData()">Load Data</button>
    <div id="result"></div>

    <script>
      function loadData() {
        let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();

        xhttp.onload = function () {
          if (this.status == 200) {
            document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = this.responseText;
          }
        };

        xhttp.open("GET", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts/1", true);
        xhttp.send();
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
```

- **Explanation:**
  - Button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá `loadData()` function call ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø AJAX request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
  - Data HTML element ‡¶è dynamically display ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, **onload** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 7. AJAX vs Fetch API

AJAX ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Fetch API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

| Feature                  | AJAX (XMLHttpRequest)                           | Fetch API                                          |
| ------------------------ | ----------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------- |
| **Syntax**               | Complex ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç verbose                             | Simple ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç cleaner                                 |
| **Response Handling**    | Callbacks ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®                              | Promise-based                                      |
| **Error Handling**       | Error handling complex                          | Easy to handle errors using `.catch()` block       |
| **Support for Promises** | No (only callbacks)                             | Yes                                                |
| **Readability**          | Less readable                                   | More readable, especially with Async/Await         |
| **Data Types**           | XML, JSON, HTML ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø format handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá | Primarily works with JSON but supports other types |

---

### 8. Conclusion

**AJAX** ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ technology, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá data transfer ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá page reload ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶á web applications ‡¶è dynamic content update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ XMLHttpRequest object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá GET ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç POST requests ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç server ‡¶è‡¶∞ response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá data dynamically display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì Fetch API ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì modern ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç cleaner syntax ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, AJAX ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§ tool‡•§

### 1. Introduction to XMLHttpRequest

**XMLHttpRequest (XHR)** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø built-in JavaScript object, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **AJAX** requests handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø web pages asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá data transfer ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ XHR ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá web page ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶´‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dynamically page ‡¶è‡¶∞ content update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

#### Key Features:

- XMLHttpRequest asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user experience ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- GET ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç POST ‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® HTTP methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Data ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® format ‡¶è handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º (JSON, XML, HTML, Text)‡•§

### 2. Why Use XMLHttpRequest?

**XMLHttpRequest** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

1. **Asynchronous Data Loading:** Page reload ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá background ‡¶è server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ server ‡¶è data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
2. **Dynamic Content Update:** Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ dynamically content update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Server Communication:** Server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá GET, POST, PUT, DELETE ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø HTTP requests ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá interaction ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
4. **Customizable Requests:** XMLHttpRequest ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ request headers, parameters, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data formats specify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

---

### 3. Creating an XMLHttpRequest Object

AJAX request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **XMLHttpRequest** object ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø XMLHttpRequest object ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ syntax ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§

##### Syntax:

```javascript
let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
```

- **Explanation:**
  - `new XMLHttpRequest()` ‡¶π‡¶≤ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø constructor, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ XMLHttpRequest object ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá data transfer ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

---

### 4. Sending a Request to the Server

XMLHttpRequest object ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ GET ‡¶¨‡¶æ POST method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá data exchange ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

#### GET Request

**GET** method ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø GET request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

##### Example:

```javascript
let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();

xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
  if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
    document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = this.responseText;
  }
};

xhttp.open("GET", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts/1", true);
xhttp.send();
```

- **Explanation:**
  - **open("GET", url, true):** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `"GET"` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `url` ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø endpoint specify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ `true` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá request asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
  - **onreadystatechange:** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø event handler, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ request ‡¶è‡¶∞ state change ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® stages handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - **this.readyState == 4:** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã request ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ `readyState` property XMLHttpRequest ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
    - **readyState Values:**
      1. **0:** Request ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡¶ø (uninitialized)
      2. **1:** Request ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá (open() ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá)
      3. **2:** Request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá (sent)
      4. **3:** Server process ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá (loading)
      5. **4:** Request ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá (done)
  - **this.status == 200:** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã request successful ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ `status == 200` HTTP status code ‡¶Ø‡¶æ success ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - **this.responseText:** Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç result HTML element ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### POST Request

**POST** method server ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® data create ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ send ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø POST request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

##### Example:

```javascript
let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();

xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
  if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 201) {
    // 201 indicates successful creation
    document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = this.responseText;
  }
};

xhttp.open("POST", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts", true);
xhttp.setRequestHeader("Content-type", "application/json");

xhttp.send(
  JSON.stringify({
    title: "foo",
    body: "bar",
    userId: 1,
  })
);
```

- **Explanation:**
  - **open("POST", url, true):** POST request ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç request asynchronous ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
  - **setRequestHeader():** Request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá content type set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé data JSON format ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
  - **send():** JSON format ‡¶è serialize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá data server ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  - **status == 201:** 201 HTTP status code ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® data ‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 5. Handling Server Responses

Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá, XMLHttpRequest object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ properties ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

#### Using onreadystatechange

**onreadystatechange** property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® state (readyState) track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ flexible ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç traditional approach‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
  if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
    document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = this.responseText;
  }
};
```

- **Explanation:**
  - Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá `readyState == 4` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `status == 200` check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá response data **responseText** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá HTML element ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### Using onload

**onload** property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ request ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ (when readyState == 4) response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `onreadystatechange` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç cleaner approach ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ request ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();

xhttp.onload = function () {
  if (this.status == 200) {
    document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = this.responseText;
  }
};

xhttp.open("GET", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts/1", true);
xhttp.send();
```

- **Explanation:**
  - **onload:** Request ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á event trigger ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ `readyState` check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ **onload** ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶á execute ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® `readyState == 4`‡•§
  - Request ‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá **status == 200** ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá response HTML ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 6. Real-life Example of XMLHttpRequest

#### With Button Click

‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá XMLHttpRequest ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá GET request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç HTML page ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>XMLHttpRequest Example</title>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>XMLHttpRequest Demo</h1>
    <button onclick="loadData()">Load Data</button>
    <div id="result"></div>

    <script>
      function loadData() {
        let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();

        xhttp.onload = function () {
          if (this.status == 200) {
            document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = this.responseText;
          }
        };

        xhttp.open("GET", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts/1", true);
        xhttp.send();
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
```

- **Explanation:**
  - Button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá `loadData()` function call ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ XMLHttpRequest ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
  - Data HTML element ‡¶è dynamically display ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, **onload** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá request ‡¶è‡¶∞ response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 7. Properties and Methods of XMLHttpRequest

XMLHttpRequest ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá table ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

| Property/Method              | Description                                                                                         |
| ---------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **open(method, url, async)** | HTTP request ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ method, URL, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç asynchronous ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§                 |
| **send(data)**               | Request send ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ GET request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `data` optional, POST ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø data ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§ |

| **setRequestHeader(header, value)**

| Request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá custom headers ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ |
| **onreadystatechange** | Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ request ‡¶è‡¶∞ state change track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ |
| **onload** | Request ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá trigger ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
| **responseText** | Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response data string ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
| **status** | HTTP response code return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 200 for success, 404 for not found‡•§ |
| **readyState** | Request ‡¶è‡¶∞ state track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ 0 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 4 ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |

---

#### Detailed Explanation and Examples:

1. **open(method, url, async)**:

   - Request ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **method** (GET, POST), **url**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **async** ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® true (asynchronous) ‡¶¨‡¶æ false (synchronous) ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

   ##### Example:

   ```javascript
   xhttp.open("GET", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts/1", true);
   ```

2. **send(data)**:

   - Request send ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ GET ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `data` optional, POST request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá `data` ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§

   ##### Example:

   ```javascript
   xhttp.send(); // GET request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø
   xhttp.send(JSON.stringify({ title: "foo", body: "bar" })); // POST request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø
   ```

3. **setRequestHeader(header, value)**:

   - Request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá custom headers ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® content type ‡¶¨‡¶æ authentication tokens‡•§

   ##### Example:

   ```javascript
   xhttp.setRequestHeader("Content-type", "application/json");
   ```

4. **onreadystatechange**:

   - Server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® state track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

   ##### Example:

   ```javascript
   xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
     if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
       console.log(this.responseText);
     }
   };
   ```

5. **onload**:

   - Request ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø trigger ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

   ##### Example:

   ```javascript
   xhttp.onload = function () {
     if (this.status == 200) {
       console.log(this.responseText);
     }
   };
   ```

6. **responseText**:

   - Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response string ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ JSON ‡¶¨‡¶æ XML data string ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

   ##### Example:

   ```javascript
   console.log(xhttp.responseText);
   ```

7. **status**:

   - Server ‡¶è‡¶∞ HTTP response code ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ **200** successful request, **404** not found‡•§

   ##### Example:

   ```javascript
   if (xhttp.status == 200) {
     console.log("Success");
   }
   ```

8. **readyState**:
   - XMLHttpRequest object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® state ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
   ##### Example:
   ```javascript
   if (xhttp.readyState == 4) {
     console.log("Request completed");
   }
   ```

### 1. Introduction to AJAX Server Response

**AJAX** (Asynchronous JavaScript and XML) ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø powerful tool, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ page reload ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá web applications ‡¶è asynchronous server requests ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® **responseText**, **responseXML**, **getResponseHeader()**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **getAllResponseHeaders()**‡•§ AJAX request ‡¶è‡¶∞ server response ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶á documentation ‡¶è ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### 2. Why Handle Server Responses?

AJAX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ Request ‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá, server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á response ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® data formats ‡¶è ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: **plain text**, **JSON**, ‡¶¨‡¶æ **XML**‡•§ Server response ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á data ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá web page ‡¶è dynamic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá content update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ AJAX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

---

### 3. Handling Server Responses

XMLHttpRequest object ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá, **responseText** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **responseXML** properties ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

#### responseText Property

**`responseText`** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø property, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã response ‡¶ï‡ßá string ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **text** ‡¶¨‡¶æ **JSON** data ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
  if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
    document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = this.responseText;
  }
};
xhttp.open("GET", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users/1", true);
xhttp.send();
```

- **Explanation:**
  - `responseText` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã **plain text** ‡¶¨‡¶æ **JSON** data string ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
  - Example ‡¶è, server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá JSON format ‡¶è data ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á data HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ **result** element ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### responseXML Property

**`responseXML`** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø property, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã response ‡¶ï‡ßá **XMLDocument object** ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø XML data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
  if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
    let xmlDoc = this.responseXML;
    let title = xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("title")[0].childNodes[0].nodeValue;
    document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = title;
  }
};
xhttp.open("GET", "https://example.com/data.xml", true);
xhttp.send();
```

- **Explanation:**
  - `responseXML` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá XML format ‡¶è data return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
  - Example ‡¶è, **XMLDocument object** ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá `<title>` tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ value retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá HTML ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 4. Fetching Response Headers

Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá response headers retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø XMLHttpRequest ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ method ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá: **getResponseHeader()** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **getAllResponseHeaders()**‡•§ Headers ‡¶π‡¶≤ additional information, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ HTTP response ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### getResponseHeader() Method

**`getResponseHeader(headerName)`** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü response header ‡¶è‡¶∞ value retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
  if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
    let contentType = xhttp.getResponseHeader("Content-Type");
    console.log("Content-Type:", contentType);
  }
};
xhttp.open("GET", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts/1", true);
xhttp.send();
```

- **Explanation:**
  - **getResponseHeader("Content-Type")** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **Content-Type** header ‡¶è‡¶∞ value retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  - Example ‡¶è, server response ‡¶è‡¶∞ content type console ‡¶è log ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ Response header ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø response ‡¶è‡¶∞ data JSON, XML, ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® format ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### getAllResponseHeaders() Method

**`getAllResponseHeaders()`** method server ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ response headers ‡¶ï‡ßá string ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø response ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ headers ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
  if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
    let headers = xhttp.getAllResponseHeaders();
    console.log("All Headers:", headers);
  }
};
xhttp.open("GET", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts/1", true);
xhttp.send();
```

- **Explanation:**
  - **getAllResponseHeaders()** server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ headers string ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - Example ‡¶è, ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ headers console ‡¶è log ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® metadata headers ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® content length, content type, server, ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

---

### 5. Real-life Example of Handling Server Responses

‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá responseText, responseXML, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç response headers handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>AJAX Server Response Example</title>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>AJAX Server Response Demo</h1>
    <button onclick="loadData()">Load Data</button>
    <div id="result"></div>

    <script>
      function loadData() {
        let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();

        xhttp.onload = function () {
          if (this.status == 200) {
            // Displaying responseText (JSON Data)
            document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = this.responseText;

            // Logging a specific response header
            let contentType = xhttp.getResponseHeader("Content-Type");
            console.log("Content-Type:", contentType);

            // Logging all response headers
            let allHeaders = xhttp.getAllResponseHeaders();
            console.log("All Headers:", allHeaders);
          }
        };

        xhttp.open("GET", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts/1", true);
        xhttp.send();
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
```

- **Explanation:**
  - Button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá **loadData()** function call ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø AJAX request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
  - **responseText** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá server response HTML element ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  - **getResponseHeader()** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá server response ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Content-Type** header console ‡¶è log ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  - **getAllResponseHeaders()** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ response headers console ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 6. Conclusion

**responseText**, **responseXML**, **getResponseHeader()**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **getAllResponseHeaders()** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã AJAX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá server response handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡•§ **responseText** server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá plain text ‡¶¨‡¶æ JSON data retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **responseXML** XML data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ **getResponseHeader()** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **getAllResponseHeaders()** methods server response ‡¶è‡¶∞ headers ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü header ‡¶è‡¶∞ value retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ AJAX ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ server ‡¶è‡¶∞ response dynamic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data display ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

## A Complete Mini Project with AJAX

#### Project Title: Fetching User Data with AJAX

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **AJAX** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá external API ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá user data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á data ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ **Sass** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá page ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá design ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ü‡¶ø absolute beginners ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

### 1. Project Overview

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **AJAX** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá [https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users](https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users) ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá user data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á data ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ web page ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø button ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá user data load ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Sass** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá page ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá design ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

### 2. Technologies Used

- **HTML**: Page structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§
- **Sass (CSS Preprocessor)**: Clean ‡¶ì modular CSS ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§
- **JavaScript (AJAX)**: Asynchronously server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

### 3. Project Structure

```
project/
‚îÇ
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ index.html             # Main HTML file
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ css/
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ style.css          # Compiled CSS from Sass
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ js/
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ script.js          # JavaScript for AJAX
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ sass/
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ _variables.scss    # Sass variables
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ _mixin.scss        # Sass mixins
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ _base.scss         # Base styles
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ main.scss          # Main Sass file that imports all
```

### 4. Writing the HTML Structure

‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá HTML structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **button** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá data load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **div** element ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### index.html

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>AJAX User Data Fetch</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css" />
  </head>
  <body>
    <div class="container">
      <h1>Fetch User Data</h1>
      <button id="loadData">Load Users</button>
      <div id="userList" class="user-list"></div>
    </div>

    <script src="js/script.js"></script>
  </body>
</html>
```

- **Explanation**:
  - ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø heading `h1` ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá page ‡¶è‡¶∞ title ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
  - ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø button ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ **id="loadData"** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶á button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá AJAX request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
  - `id="userList"` ‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø div ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ data display ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### 5. Setting up Sass Folder Structure

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Sass ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø clean structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ variables, mixins ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç base styles ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ file ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ `main.scss` ‡¶è import ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§

#### sass/\_variables.scss

```scss
// Color variables
$primary-color: #3498db;
$secondary-color: #2ecc71;
$font-color: #ffffff;
$background-color: #f5f5f5;
```

#### sass/\_mixin.scss

```scss
// Mixin for buttons
@mixin button-styles($bg-color, $font-color) {
  padding: 10px 20px;
  background-color: $bg-color;
  color: $font-color;
  border: none;
  border-radius: 5px;
  cursor: pointer;
  font-size: 16px;

  &:hover {
    background-color: darken($bg-color, 10%);
  }
}
```

#### sass/\_base.scss

```scss
// Base styles
* {
  margin: 0;
  padding: 0;
  box-sizing: border-box;
}

body {
  font-family: Arial, sans-serif;
  background-color: $background-color;
}

.container {
  max-width: 600px;
  margin: 50px auto;
  padding: 20px;
  background-color: $font-color;
  border-radius: 8px;
  box-shadow: 0 0 10px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);
  text-align: center;
}
```

#### sass/main.scss

```scss
// Importing all Sass partials
@import "variables";
@import "mixin";
@import "base";

// Button styling
button {
  @include button-styles($primary-color, $font-color);
}

.user-list {
  margin-top: 20px;
  padding: 10px;
  background-color: $secondary-color;
  border-radius: 5px;
  color: $font-color;
}
```

- **Explanation**:
  - **\_variables.scss**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá color variables define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ styles ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§
  - **\_mixin.scss**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá button ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø reusable mixin ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  - **\_base.scss**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ default/base styles ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® margin, padding reset ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç container ‡¶è‡¶∞ design handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - **main.scss**: ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ `main.scss` ‡¶è import ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç button ‡¶ì user list ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø additional styles ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 6. Using Sass for Styling

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Sass ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá page ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá design ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Sass file ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá styling ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ code ‡¶ï‡ßá clean ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainable ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### 7. Writing the JavaScript with AJAX

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **JavaScript** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **AJAX** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á data dynamically display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§

#### js/script.js

```javascript
document.getElementById("loadData").addEventListener("click", loadUserData);

function loadUserData() {
  let xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();

  xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
    if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
      const users = JSON.parse(this.responseText);
      let output = "";

      users.forEach((user) => {
        output += `
          <div class="user-card">
            <h3>${user.name}</h3>
            <p>Email: ${user.email}</p>
            <p>Phone: ${user.phone}</p>
          </div>
        `;
      });

      document.getElementById("userList").innerHTML = output;
    }
  };

  xhttp.open("GET", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users", true);
  xhttp.send();
}
```

- **Explanation**:
  - Button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶á **loadUserData** function call ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **AJAX** request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JSON format ‡¶è data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
  - **onreadystatechange** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá response ready ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá user data display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
  - **users.forEach()** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø user data HTML structure ‡¶è dynamically convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 8. Putting It All Together

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **AJAX** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Sass** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç interactive page ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§ Button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá user data fetch ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá HTML structure ‡¶è display ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### 9. Conclusion

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá **AJAX** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á data ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá dynamically display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ì, **Sass** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá project ‡¶ï‡ßá clean ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modular ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### 1. Introduction to jQuery and JavaScript

**JavaScript** ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø powerful ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç essential scripting language, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ browser ‡¶è run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **DOM manipulation**, **event handling**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **AJAX** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**jQuery**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ 2006 ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤, JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø library ‡¶Ø‡¶æ DOM manipulation ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø common tasks (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® event handling, animations, AJAX requests) ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï feature ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç browser compatibility ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á **jQuery** developer ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡•§

‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá, **2024** ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ (ES6+) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç improved browser support ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá jQuery ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® vanilla JavaScript ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Source: [W3Schools - jQuery Selectors](https://www.w3schools.com/js/js_jquery_selectors.asp)

---

### 2. Key Differences Between jQuery and JavaScript

| Feature                   | JavaScript                                         | jQuery                                                    |
| ------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Syntax**                | Complex and sometimes lengthy                      | Short and concise                                         |
| **DOM Manipulation**      | Native methods are longer and more manual          | Simplified and easy-to-use functions                      |
| **Event Handling**        | Requires `addEventListener()` with specific syntax | `$().on()` or shorthand methods like `click()`, `hover()` |
| **Browser Compatibility** | Modern browsers handle JavaScript consistently     | Initially used for cross-browser compatibility            |
| **Performance**           | Faster for simple tasks (native execution)         | Slightly slower due to library overhead                   |
| **AJAX Handling**         | Uses `XMLHttpRequest` or `fetch`                   | Simplified with `$.ajax()` and shorthand methods          |
| **Size**                  | No extra files, native to browser                  | Requires adding an external library                       |

---

### 3. Simplifying DOM Manipulation

#### DOM Manipulation in JavaScript

JavaScript ‡¶è DOM manipulation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ built-in methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ lengthy ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá modern JavaScript (ES6+) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example (JavaScript):

```javascript
// JavaScript to hide an element
document.getElementById("myElement").style.display = "none";

// JavaScript to change multiple elements' color
const elements = document.querySelectorAll(".myClass");
elements.forEach((el) => (el.style.color = "blue"));
```

#### DOM Manipulation in jQuery

**jQuery** DOM manipulation ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ jQuery ‡¶è‡¶∞ selectors ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example (jQuery):

```javascript
// jQuery to hide an element
$("#myElement").hide();

// jQuery to change multiple elements' color
$(".myClass").css("color", "blue");
```

- **Explanation**:
  - JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º jQuery ‡¶è‡¶∞ syntax ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡•§ `#` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `.` selector ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ elements manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
  - ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá modern JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ `querySelectorAll()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á multiple elements select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 4. Event Handling

#### Event Handling in JavaScript

JavaScript ‡¶è event handling ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `addEventListener()` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì syntax ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ flexible ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modern browser support ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶á method ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® widely accepted.

##### Example (JavaScript):

```javascript
document.getElementById("myButton").addEventListener("click", function () {
  alert("Button Clicked!");
});
```

#### Event Handling in jQuery

jQuery ‡¶§‡ßá event handling ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø shorthand methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `click()` ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ `hover()` method.

##### Example (jQuery):

```javascript
$("#myButton").click(function () {
  alert("Button Clicked!");
});
```

- **Explanation**:
  - jQuery ‡¶è‡¶∞ **shorthand** method ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã event handling ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá modern JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ **addEventListener** method ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá browser compatibility support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì maintainable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

---

### 5. AJAX Requests

#### AJAX with JavaScript

AJAX request ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá **XMLHttpRequest** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá modern browsers ‡¶è **Fetch API** ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

##### Example (Using Fetch API in JavaScript):

```javascript
fetch("https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users")
  .then((response) => response.json())
  .then((data) => {
    console.log(data);
  })
  .catch((error) => console.log("Error:", error));
```

#### AJAX with jQuery

jQuery ‡¶§‡ßá AJAX request ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `.ajax()`, `.get()`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `.post()` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã shorthand methods ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example (jQuery):

```javascript
$.get("https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users", function (data) {
  console.log(data);
});
```

- **Explanation**:
  - **jQuery** AJAX requests ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® modern JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Fetch API** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú, powerful ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 6. Why You Shouldn‚Äôt Use jQuery in 2024

**2024** ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá, jQuery ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

#### 1. **Modern JavaScript is Powerful Enough**:

Modern JavaScript (ES6+) ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï powerful ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç expressive‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø JavaScript ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á jQuery ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã tasks handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§ Features like:

- **querySelector() / querySelectorAll()** DOM elements select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá,
- **Fetch API** AJAX requests handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá,
- **Arrow functions** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Promises** asynchronous operations ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç clean ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### 2. **Library Overhead**:

jQuery ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø external library ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ project ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **extra file** ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ page ‡¶è‡¶∞ load time ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Modern JavaScript ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá jQuery ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá library add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ overhead ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 3. **Browser Compatibility Issues No Longer a Concern**:

jQuery ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø browser compatibility issues handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Internet Explorer ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßá JavaScript functionality ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ major browsers (Chrome, Firefox, Edge) modern JavaScript features ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶á support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á compatibility ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§

#### 4. **Performance Considerations**:

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ native execution, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé **vanilla JavaScript**, jQuery ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º fast‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ jQuery ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø library, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ **extra overhead** ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ project ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø DOM manipulation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá JavaScript directly ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá performance ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 5. **Learning Modern JavaScript**:

Modern JavaScript (ES6+) ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ developer ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶Å‡¶°‡¶º‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï libraries ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç frameworks (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® React, Vue) modern JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á jQuery ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá vanilla JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ES6 ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§

#### 6. **Other Modern Libraries**:

React, Vue.js ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã modern libraries ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç frameworks DOM manipulation ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç event handling ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø efficient ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç scalable solution ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã web applications ‡¶è **component-based** development introduce ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ jQuery ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã approach ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 7. Conclusion

**JavaScript** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **jQuery** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ **2024** ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá jQuery ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ Modern JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶§‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á powerful ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá DOM manipulation, event handling, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç AJAX requests ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶ì jQuery ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã legacy project ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á jQuery ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® projects ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø modern JavaScript ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø practical ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

**2024** ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø jQuery ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶Ç modern JavaScript (ES6+) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ñ‡¶≤ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

## What is JavaScript Library

JavaScript Library ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **pre-written JavaScript code** ‡¶è‡¶∞ collection, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ì ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá, library ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### JavaScript Library ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø:

1. **Pre-written Code**: Libraries ‡¶è ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®, ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶•‡¶° ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Code Reusability**: ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá library ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ì ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
3. **Simplified Syntax**: ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá library ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
4. **Cross-browser Compatibility**: JavaScript libraries ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá compatibility ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º JavaScript Libraries:

1. **jQuery**: DOM manipulation, event handling, and animations ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
2. **Lodash**: JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ arrays, objects, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç strings ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï utility functions ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
3. **Moment.js**: Date ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç time ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
4. **D3.js**: Data-driven documents ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ visualization ‡¶¨‡¶æ data visualizations ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

### ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá JavaScript Library ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º?

1. ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø HTML ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá `<script>` ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá CDN ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø library ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§
2. ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø NPM (Node Package Manager) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

```html
<!-- Example: jQuery CDN -->
<script src="https://ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/jquery/3.5.1/jquery.min.js"></script>

<script>
  $(document).ready(function () {
    $("p").click(function () {
      $(this).hide();
    });
  });
</script>
```

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ jQuery ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ event handling ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá paragraph ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶° ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
